The Separatists' portrayal of the Jedi largely succeeded in maligning their character in the eyes of the public, as few in the Confederacy knew that the Order was not given a choice in the matter. It was the Order's preference to not be used as icons of heroism, having long resisted attempts at romanticizing the Jedi, especially for the purpose of wartime propaganda. The Jedi, therefore, were mostly absent from galactic culture, which allowed anti-Jedi sentiment to grow from preconceptions instead of a genuine rebuttal of the Order's practices. The Separatists were convinced that the Order neglected their worlds, forcing them to secede from the Republic. Separatist civilians conflated the Order with the [Core Worlds](/wiki/Core_Worlds "Core Worlds")' reputation for cultural elitism, and some even viewed the Jedi as "[evil](/wiki/Deliver_Us_From_Jedi_Evil "Deliver Us From Jedi Evil")" and a fanatical sect of "warmongers." The historian [Janyor](/wiki/Janyor "Janyor") theorized that such misconceptions of the Jedi could have been averted if the Order had been more engaged with the populace.[[125]](#cite_note-Propaganda-125)

Anti-Jedi sentiment was openly espoused by the Republic's successor, the [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire").[[125]](#cite_note-Propaganda-125) The self-proclaimed [Galactic Emperor](/wiki/Galactic_Emperor "Galactic Emperor") Sheev Palpatine accused the entire Order of [treason](/wiki/Treason "Treason"), maligning the Order's reputation[[49]](#cite_note-Catalyst-49) after several members of the High Council, having discovered his true identity as a Sith, attempted to [arrest the chancellor](/wiki/Duel_in_Palpatine%27s_office "Duel in Palpatine's office").[[19]](#cite_note-Episode_III-19) Palpatine squarely blamed the Jedi for recent troubles[[134]](#cite_note-Launchpad229-134) and accused them of using their "mystical powers" to cause the Clone War[[124]](#cite_note-Crimson_Reign_3-124) in order to secure power. [Grand Vizier](/wiki/Grand_Vizier "Grand Vizier") [Mas Amedda](/wiki/Mas_Amedda "Mas Amedda") publicly [denounced](/wiki/Celebration_marking_the_eradication_of_the_Jedi_Order "Celebration marking the eradication of the Jedi Order") the Order as a symbol of fear and referred to the Order's downfall as the beginning of a new "age of freedom."[[135]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_1-135) With the exception of individuals like Lyra Erso, the Order was effectively forgotten by the galaxy during the early days of the [Imperial Era](/wiki/Imperial_Era "Imperial Era")[[49]](#cite_note-Catalyst-49) as the Empire quickly moved to cover up its existence.[[124]](#cite_note-Crimson_Reign_3-124) Despite the [Alliance to Restore the Republic](/wiki/Alliance_to_Restore_the_Republic "Alliance to Restore the Republic") largely having pro-Jedi views,[[136]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_(2020)_26-136) its individual members were not immune to the era's bias, with soldier [Reyé Hollis](/wiki/Rey%C3%A9_Hollis "Reyé Hollis") believing stories he heard of the Jedi being ineffective fools who stole glory for themselves.[[137]](#cite_note-Luke_on_the_Bright_Side-137)

###### Collapse in public opinion[]

:   "*Aren't you a bit busy with your war to be bothering with the likes of us?*"
:   ―[Tiggs Leo](/wiki/Tiggs_Leo "Tiggs Leo")[[138]](#cite_note-Lethal_Trackdown-138)

In general, Republic citizens were unaware of the Order's motives for fighting in the Clone Wars. To some individuals,[[125]](#cite_note-Propaganda-125) such as the Mandalorian [Duchess](/wiki/Duchess "Duchess") [Satine Kryze](/wiki/Satine_Kryze "Satine Kryze")[[102]](#cite_note-VoT-102) or the [Coruscanti](/wiki/Coruscanti "Coruscanti") civilian [Letta Turmond](/wiki/Letta_Turmond "Letta Turmond"), the Jedi had forsaken their principles as peacekeepers by becoming military leaders and battlefield warriors.[[139]](#cite_note-The_Jedi_Who_Knew_Too_Much-139) [Tee Watt Kaa](/wiki/Tee_Watt_Kaa "Tee Watt Kaa"), the head of a [Lurmen village](/wiki/Lurmen_village "Lurmen village") on [Maridun](/wiki/Maridun "Maridun"), rejected the argument that the Jedi were peacekeepers, a function that he believed was incompatible with the Order's participation in the Clone Wars.[[106]](#cite_note-Jedi_Crash-106) A committed, to the death, pacifist, Kaa was unwilling to compromise his views, refusing to permit the other [Lurmens](/wiki/Lurmen "Lurmen") to defend their village against the [Confederacy military](/wiki/Confederacy_military "Confederacy military"). They ultimately defied Kaa's authority upon witnessing the Jedi's efforts to [save the Lurmens](/wiki/Defense_of_Maridun "Defense of Maridun") from [extermination](/wiki/Defoliator "Defoliator") by General [Lok Durd](/wiki/Lok_Durd "Lok Durd").[[140]](#cite_note-DoP-140)

 [![When the Jedi became military generals during the last years of the Republic, many took them as warmongers who had abandoned their peacekeeping mission.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cc/Tiplar_and_Doom_marines.png/revision/latest?cb=20200226152338) [![When the Jedi became military generals during the last years of the Republic, many took them as warmongers who had abandoned their peacekeeping mission.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cc/Tiplar_and_Doom_marines.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20200226152338)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cc/Tiplar_and_Doom_marines.png/revision/latest?cb=20200226152338) 

When the Jedi became military generals during the last years of the Republic, many took them as warmongers who had abandoned their peacekeeping mission.

 

At the height of the Clone Wars, people throughout the galaxy regarded the Jedi as warmongers, particularly in territories controlled by the [Confederacy of Independent Systems](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems "Confederacy of Independent Systems"). However, most beings did not know that the Order went to war to honor its commitment to protect the Senate, the Republic,[[125]](#cite_note-Propaganda-125) and the galaxy at large.[[141]](#cite_note-Mace_Windu_5-141) Nevertheless, the Clone Wars caused civilians[[142]](#cite_note-Old_Friends-142) like Turmond[[139]](#cite_note-The_Jedi_Who_Knew_Too_Much-139) and the Martez sisters to lose faith in the Order.[[143]](#cite_note-Raffa_DB-143) Rafa Martez and her sister, Trace Martez, faulted the Order for the deaths of their parents when a Jedi had redirected a transport from a platform of people, only for it to hit their apartment. With the Jedi seemingly uncompassionate towards their plight, the sisters found themselves left alone and with anger at the Jedi.[[82]](#cite_note-Dangerous_Debt-82)

While Separatists were opposed to the Jedi due to their allegiance with the Republic, with many of [Lux Bonteri](/wiki/Lux_Bonteri "Lux Bonteri")'s friends blaming the Jedi for the bloodshed of the Clone Wars,[[144]](#cite_note-Heroes_on_Both_Sides-144) the citizens of the Republic would turn on the Jedi due to losing faith in their Order. To the public, the Jedi looked like a force who seemed more interested in playing politics[[142]](#cite_note-Old_Friends-142) or waging war[[138]](#cite_note-Lethal_Trackdown-138) than helping those in danger[[142]](#cite_note-Old_Friends-142) or need.[[145]](#cite_note-Gone_with_a_Trace-145) Indeed, in focusing on the Clone Wars, the Jedi had less time to aid the people of the Republic they were meant to protect.[[138]](#cite_note-Lethal_Trackdown-138) Trace Martez thought of the Jedi as a police force who started the war and had forgotten about the less well off citizens of Coruscant.[[145]](#cite_note-Gone_with_a_Trace-145) While a concern about the political ramifications of their actions could be seen in the late High Republic Era,[[146]](#cite_note-LostFound-146) former Jedi Ahsoka Tano believed that the Jedi of the Clone Wars era had overwhelmingly tied themselves to the Republic's political state, with Tano herself only regaining her faith in the Jedi when she was reminded of how important the Order could be when it helped those in need. Even then, she made sure to criticize what she regarded as political chess playing on the Order's part when again confronted by it.[[142]](#cite_note-Old_Friends-142)

##### Late Republic pro-Jedi views[]

:   "*But at what cost? It's like you once said. Many lives get caught between the Republic and the Separatists.*"  
    "*I did say that once, but after watching the heroics and selflessness of the Jedi, I do believe the Republic is the right side to be on.*"
:   ―Ahsoka Tano and Lux Bonteri[[147]](#cite_note-Tipping_Points-147)

 [![Lyra Erso was a spiritual woman who supported the Jedi Order out of reverence of the Force.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2c/Lyra_Erso-RO-Collectors_Edition-Titan.png/revision/latest?cb=20230728041234) [![Lyra Erso was a spiritual woman who supported the Jedi Order out of reverence of the Force.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2c/Lyra_Erso-RO-Collectors_Edition-Titan.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20230728041234)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2c/Lyra_Erso-RO-Collectors_Edition-Titan.png/revision/latest?cb=20230728041234) 

Lyra Erso was a spiritual woman who supported the Jedi Order out of reverence of the Force.

 

Prior to the Clone Wars, the people of the Galactic Republic kept faith with the Jedi Order[[148]](#cite_note-AoR-Maul-148) that had acquitted itself through a thousand years of loyal service.[[20]](#cite_note-TSWB-20) [Lyra Erso](/wiki/Lyra_Erso "Lyra Erso"), the [wife](/wiki/Marriage "Marriage") of [Doctor](/wiki/Doctor "Doctor") [Galen Walton Erso](/wiki/Galen_Walton_Erso "Galen Walton Erso"), supported the Order's views on charity, compassion, and peace. Erso's support for the Order was rooted in her faith in the Force, which evolved from her lifelong love of nature, and her belief in the concepts of good and evil. The Force, as Erso viewed it, was the epitome of perfection and good. During the Clone Wars, Erso believed that the Order was the Republic's best defense against the "powers of evil." Erso also admired the Jedi Temple on Coruscant for its elegance and location on a Force nexus. She often exercised on the Temple grounds prior to the Clone Wars; after the conflict began, however, Erso noticed a changed atmosphere at the now heavily patrolled [temple district](/wiki/Palace_Court "Palace Court"), which made the area virtually inaccessible to the public with the exception of individuals who carried high security clearance.[[49]](#cite_note-Catalyst-49)

Erso's [pregnancy](/wiki/Reproduction "Reproduction") was the closest she felt to experiencing the Force in the way that she imagined the Jedi's connection to it—an incomprehensible and "profound connection with life." She recognized the Force as the source of the Jedi's power, granting them abilities that far exceeded Erso's strengths and intuition. However, she comforted herself with the belief that while she could not use the Force as the Jedi could, she was able to sense it nonetheless. In the aftermath of the [Order 66](/wiki/Order_66 "Order 66"), Erso rejected the Galactic Empire's explanation for the [Great Jedi Purge](/wiki/Great_Jedi_Purge "Great Jedi Purge"), refusing to believe that the Jedi betrayed the Republic. Whereas the public generally accepted the deaths of thousands of Jedi, largely out of relief over the end of the Clone Wars, Erso was heartbroken by the Order's destruction and cried for [hours](/wiki/Standard_hour "Standard hour") as a result, an experience she likened to the loss of a family member. Despite the eradication of the Order, Erso continued to believe in the Jedi whose principles influenced her sense of morality.[[49]](#cite_note-Catalyst-49)

 [![Though a former Separatist, Lux Bonteri grew to see the Jedi as heroes for their role in the liberation of Onderon.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1f/Saw_Lux_Anakin_Ahsoka_Jedi_Temple.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161215090135) [![Though a former Separatist, Lux Bonteri grew to see the Jedi as heroes for their role in the liberation of Onderon.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1f/Saw_Lux_Anakin_Ahsoka_Jedi_Temple.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161215090135)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1f/Saw_Lux_Anakin_Ahsoka_Jedi_Temple.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161215090135) 

Though a former Separatist, Lux Bonteri grew to see the Jedi as heroes for their role in the liberation of Onderon.

 

In addition to Erso,[[49]](#cite_note-Catalyst-49) the Jedi's deeds won the respect and admiration of individuals who worked closely with the Order, such as [Cham Syndulla](/wiki/Cham_Syndulla "Cham Syndulla")[[149]](#cite_note-SWR:Homecoming-149) and [Lux Bonteri](/wiki/Lux_Bonteri "Lux Bonteri").[[147]](#cite_note-Tipping_Points-147) During the [Battle of Ryloth](/wiki/Battle_of_Ryloth "Battle of Ryloth") of the Clone War, Syndulla was initially hesitant to accept the Order's offer of an alliance between the [Grand Army of the Republic](/wiki/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic "Grand Army of the Republic") and the [Twi'lek Resistance](/wiki/Twi%27lek_Resistance "Twi'lek Resistance"), knowing that the Republic would occupy [Ryloth](/wiki/Ryloth "Ryloth") in the battle's aftermath.[[150]](#cite_note-Liberty_on_Ryloth-150) Ultimately, though, Syndulla developed a newfound respect of the Jedi for their role in the liberation of his homeworld, particularly [Jedi General](/wiki/Jedi_General "Jedi General") [Mace Windu](/wiki/Mace_Windu "Mace Windu"), whose memory the [Twi'leks](/wiki/Twi%27lek "Twi'lek") honored in songs dedicated to the liberation of their [homeworld](/wiki/Homeworld "Homeworld").[[149]](#cite_note-SWR:Homecoming-149) Bonteri worked with the Order during the [Onderonian Civil War](/wiki/Onderonian_Civil_War "Onderonian Civil War"),[[147]](#cite_note-Tipping_Points-147) having joined the [Onderon rebels](/wiki/Onderon_rebels "Onderon rebels") after his [mother](/wiki/House_Bonteri "House Bonteri"), [Separatist Senator](/wiki/Separatist_Senate "Separatist Senate") [Mina Bonteri](/wiki/Mina_Bonteri "Mina Bonteri"), was [assassinated](/wiki/Assassin "Assassin") at the behest of Count Dooku.[[151]](#cite_note-Lux_Bonteri_DB-151) By training and fighting alongside the Onderon rebels, the Jedi changed Bonteri's views on the Republic and the Order. Inspired by the selflessness and heroism of the Order, Bonteri vowed to restore the union between [Onderon](/wiki/Onderon "Onderon") and the Republic.[[147]](#cite_note-Tipping_Points-147)

## History[]

### Ancient times[]

:   "*For over a thousand generations the Jedi Knights were the guardians of peace and justice in the Old Republic. Before the dark times. Before the Empire.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi[[44]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-44)

 [![The Jedi Order began with the Prime Jedi a thousand generations before the Battle of Yavin.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3e/Prime_Jedi.png/revision/latest?cb=20220413031517) [![The Jedi Order began with the Prime Jedi a thousand generations before the Battle of Yavin.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3e/Prime_Jedi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20220413031517)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3e/Prime_Jedi.png/revision/latest?cb=20220413031517) 

The Jedi Order began with the Prime Jedi a thousand generations before the Battle of Yavin.

 

The precursors of the Jedi were the [Dai Bendu](/wiki/Dai_Bendu "Dai Bendu"),[[152]](#cite_note-Unlimited_Power-152) but the Jedi Order itself was founded in the distant past on planet Ahch-To by the Prime Jedi[[14]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-14) in [25,025 BBY](/wiki/25,025_BBY "25,025 BBY").[[15]](#cite_note-GalacticAtlasNew-15) According to the legend, [Force-imbued swords](/wiki/Force-imbued_sword "Force-imbued sword") were used prior to invention of the lightsaber by the earlier Force adepts and the Jedi Order.[[153]](#cite_note-NoP-153) At the dawn of their order, the Jedi came into possession of Ilum, an ancient planet encased in [ice](/wiki/Water "Water") and littered with kyber crystals, the heart of the Jedi lightsaber. Considered the Jedi Order's most sacred world, its ancient Temple would eventually host the Gathering, a tradition that would continue up until the fall of the Order.[[54]](#cite_note-DB:Ilum-54) As the Jedi were spread throughout the galaxy, they acquired a vessel called the *[Crucible](/wiki/Crucible "Crucible")* that would ferry students to Ilum so that they could perform the Gathering. It would become the base of the [architect droid](/wiki/Architect_droid "Architect droid"), [Professor](/wiki/Professor "Professor") [Huyang](/wiki/Huyang "Huyang"), for over a thousand [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") as he instructed on lightsaber designs and kept records of every single Jedi weapon created.[[33]](#cite_note-The_Gathering-33)[[154]](#cite_note-:1-154) During this early period, the Order also established itself on Ossus, Jedha, [Xenxiar](/wiki/Xenxiar "Xenxiar"), and other worlds.[[155]](#cite_note-TROS_JN-155) Later, some Jedi [scholars](/wiki/Scholar "Scholar") argued that a number of locations could be considered the birthplace of the Order. The scholars argued that Coruscant, Jedha, and Ossus as well as worlds shrouded in myth, such as Tython and Ahch-To could all be considered candidate worlds for the Order's birth and the location of the first Jedi temple.[[6]](#cite_note-CL_2016-6)

The Jedi religion, as it was called by Luke Skywalker,[[18]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-18) was based around eight "sacred texts" that "describe tenets, history, and specific guidance to those studying the path of the Jedi." These texts included the *Rammahgon* and the *[Aionomica](/wiki/Aionomica "Aionomica")*—separated into two volumes, *Aionomicum I* and *Aionomicum II*. These books included a number of aspects of the Jedi religion that appeared to have little influence on later Jedi, such as references to "gods" and the [World Between Worlds](/wiki/World_Between_Worlds "World Between Worlds"). They also included more mundane information, such as lightsaber designs. The theology of the Jedi religion changed over time; many Jedi, such as Master [Odan-Urr](/wiki/Odan-Urr "Odan-Urr"), annotated even the sacred texts. Much was added to the Jedi canon over time, giving rise to the belief that the *Aionomicum II* doubled in size during its compilation.[[65]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-65) The fortunes of the Jedi waxed and waned over the centuries; multiple times throughout its long history, the Order had been reduced to a mere handful of adherents. [[28]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-28)

At some point prior to around [20,000 BBY](/wiki/20,000_BBY "20,000 BBY"),[[156]](#cite_note-Ordu_Date-156) a Jedi sect known as the [Ordu Aspectu](/wiki/Ordu_Aspectu "Ordu Aspectu") broke off from the Jedi Order. Led by the enigmatic [Rur](/wiki/Rur "Rur") and his second in command, [Amon](/wiki/Amon "Amon"), they sought to achieve the secrets to immortality. Eventually, a [conflict](/wiki/Entruvia_Conflict "Entruvia Conflict") broke out between them and the orthodox Jedi. The conflict ended with the signing of a [peace treaty](/wiki/Jedi%E2%80%93Ordu_Aspectu_treaty "Jedi–Ordu Aspectu treaty"). The treaty allowed the Ordu Aspectu to continue their research but under Jedi scrutiny. During his experimentation, Rur attempted to copy his intellect into his [citadel's](/wiki/Citadel_of_Rur "Citadel of Rur") computer core, only to accidentally transfer his very sentience as well. When the Jedi sought to investigate the computer closer[[12]](#cite_note-Doctor_Aphra_6-12) around 20,000 BBY,[[156]](#cite_note-Ordu_Date-156) the computer activated the citadel's security droids, [killing all members](/wiki/Attack_on_Garn "Attack on Garn") of the Ordu Aspectu and Jedi alike; but not before it was deactivated by Rur and Amon before they died themselves, thus ending the Ordu Aspectu.[[12]](#cite_note-Doctor_Aphra_6-12)

 [![The Hundred-Year Darkness saw a schism within the Jedi Order, with the followers of the dark side becoming known as the Sith.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a5/JediVsSith-SOTS.png/revision/latest?cb=20220502004842) [![The Hundred-Year Darkness saw a schism within the Jedi Order, with the followers of the dark side becoming known as the Sith.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a5/JediVsSith-SOTS.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220502004842)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a5/JediVsSith-SOTS.png/revision/latest?cb=20220502004842) 

The Hundred-Year Darkness saw a schism within the Jedi Order, with the followers of the dark side becoming known as the Sith.

 

The Sith and the Jedi were once considered "brothers" in the Force prior to the [Hundred-Year Darkness](/wiki/Hundred-Year_Darkness "Hundred-Year Darkness"), from which the Sith Order was born.[[74]](#cite_note-SW9-74) A [rogue Jedi](/wiki/Unidentified_rogue_Jedi "Unidentified rogue Jedi") had come to believe that the true power of the Force lay not in contemplation and passivity,[[13]](#cite_note-swe-Sith-13) and instead sought abandon and strength through the dark side of the Force.[[157]](#cite_note-swe-Order-157) The Jedi High Council at the time balked at this new direction, and the fallen Jedi was cast out of the Order's ranks. In spite of his banishment, the outcast gained followers to his new order. The power-hungry[[13]](#cite_note-swe-Sith-13) Sith sought to control the galaxy and opposed the Jedi, against whom they waged a series of wars which brought destruction to many worlds, including the Sith homeworld of [Moraband](/wiki/Moraband "Moraband"), which the Sith were eventually forced to abandon.[[158]](#cite_note-Sacrifice-158) On another occasion, the Jedi Order and the Sith fought a [battle](/wiki/Battle_of_Takodana_(Jedi_versus_Sith) "Battle of Takodana (Jedi versus Sith)") on the planet [Takodana](/wiki/Takodana "Takodana").[[159]](#cite_note-tfa-TVD-159) These wars also saw the construction of ancient [superweapons](/wiki/Superweapon "Superweapon") powered by giant kyber crystals which possessed the power to destroy entire planets. These weapons, along with the crystals, were destroyed and a thousand years later believed by many Jedi to be merely legends.[[160]](#cite_note-TBB-160)

About five-thousand years before the [Battle of Yavin](/wiki/Battle_of_Yavin "Battle of Yavin"),[[70]](#cite_note-Tarkin-70) the Order eventually came to be headquartered at Coruscant, wherein they built a Temple that would pose as their main hub for thousands of generations.[[161]](#cite_note-swe-Temple-161) Underneath the structure lay buried an ancient [Sith shrine](/wiki/Shrine_in_the_Depths "Shrine in the Depths"), the inherent power of which was believed by the contemporary Jedi to have been neutralized and successfully capped. In truth, that power had seeped upward and outward since its entombment, infiltrating the hallways and rooms above, and weakening the Jedi Order for millennia without their knowledge.[[70]](#cite_note-Tarkin-70)

 [![The Jedi Knights protected the galaxy as the guardians of peace and justice since the time of the Old Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/da/OldRepublicEmblem.svg/revision/latest?cb=20250720043825) [![The Jedi Knights protected the galaxy as the guardians of peace and justice since the time of the Old Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/da/OldRepublicEmblem.svg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250720043825)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/da/OldRepublicEmblem.svg/revision/latest?cb=20250720043825) 

The Jedi Knights protected the galaxy as the guardians of peace and justice since the time of the Old Republic.

 

It was during this time that the Jedi Order came into the service of what would be later called the Old Republic. Promising to uphold its ideals, the Jedi fought to maintain peace and freedom. When the Old Republic outlawed slavery, the Jedi set about to free those held, notably under the [Zygerrian Slave Empire](/wiki/Zygerrian_Slave_Empire "Zygerrian Slave Empire"). The Jedi declared war on [Zygerrians](/wiki/Zygerrian "Zygerrian"), whose economic success had resulted from enslaving beings from all corners of the galaxy before selling them at auctions. The Jedi Order managed to put an end to their practices, destroying their empire and exiling them to their homeworld, [Zygerria](/wiki/Zygerria "Zygerria"). The Zygerrians developed a fierce hatred for the Jedi as a result.[[133]](#cite_note-Kidnapped-133)[[162]](#cite_note-Slaves_of_the_Republic-162)[[163]](#cite_note-Escape_from_Kadavo-163)

[Conflicts](/wiki/Mandalorian-Jedi_War "Mandalorian-Jedi War") also arose between the Jedi and the inhabitants of the world of [Mandalore](/wiki/Mandalore "Mandalore") who had rapidly developed into a warlike culture in which strength was valued above all else. Their beliefs of continual warfare went contrary to the Jedi's mission of protecting the weak, they quickly mobilized to stop the destructive Mandalorians from expanding in the galaxy. The constant warfare was a strain and, as the Old Republic crumbled, the Mandalorian warriors sacked the Jedi Temple on Coruscant, an event during which [Pre Vizsla](/wiki/Pre_Vizsla "Pre Vizsla")'s ancestors stole the [Darksaber](/wiki/Darksaber "Darksaber").[[29]](#cite_note-TMP-29)

 [![Though defeated by the Jedi, the Sith would survive for centuries as a result of Darth Bane's reforms.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e1/Darth_Bane_TCW.png/revision/latest?cb=20140701230520) [![Though defeated by the Jedi, the Sith would survive for centuries as a result of Darth Bane's reforms.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e1/Darth_Bane_TCW.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140701230520)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e1/Darth_Bane_TCW.png/revision/latest?cb=20140701230520) 

Though defeated by the Jedi, the Sith would survive for centuries as a result of Darth Bane's reforms.

 

Prior to [1032 BBY](/wiki/1032_BBY "1032 BBY"),[[164]](#cite_note-Fall_date-164) the galaxy entered an era known as the [Dark Age](/wiki/Fall_of_the_Old_Republic "Fall of the Old Republic"). During this time the [Jedi-Sith War](/wiki/Jedi-Sith_War "Jedi-Sith War") occurred. Early on in the war, the Sith [attacked](/wiki/Battle_of_Coruscant_(Jedi-Sith_War) "Battle of Coruscant (Jedi-Sith War)") and captured Coruscant and with it the Jedi Temple. Towards the end of the war the Jedi reclaimed the Republic capital and their temple during the [liberation of Coruscant](/wiki/Liberation_of_Coruscant "Liberation of Coruscant").[[125]](#cite_note-Propaganda-125)

Even as the Old Republic collapsed, the Jedi emerged victorious from their wars with the Sith.[[125]](#cite_note-Propaganda-125) In their constant thirst for power, the Sith had weakened themselves through infighting,[[158]](#cite_note-Sacrifice-158) which allowed the Jedi to defeat the weakened Sith.[[165]](#cite_note-DB:Bane-165) Unbeknownst to the Jedi at the time, [Darth Bane](/wiki/Darth_Bane "Darth Bane") remained as the sole surviving [Dark Lord of the Sith](/wiki/Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith "Dark Lord of the Sith"). As a result of the infighting that weakened the Sith,[[158]](#cite_note-Sacrifice-158) Jedi Knights[[166]](#cite_note-Bane_Galactic_Files-166) were able to [defeat](/wiki/Defeat_of_the_Sith "Defeat of the Sith") the Sith at[[70]](#cite_note-Tarkin-70) the [Mid Rim](/wiki/Mid_Rim_Territories "Mid Rim Territories") planet[[167]](#cite_note-Visual_Encyclopedia-167) [Ruusan](/wiki/Ruusan "Ruusan")[[168]](#cite_note-Helmet_Collection-168) This confrontation nearly destroyed the ancient Sith Order,[[165]](#cite_note-DB:Bane-165) and forced the Sith to go into hiding.[[70]](#cite_note-Tarkin-70) After this, Bane established the [Rule of Two](/wiki/Rule_of_Two "Rule of Two"), declaring that the Sith thenceforth would consist of a [Sith Master](/wiki/Sith_Master "Sith Master") and a [Sith apprentice](/wiki/Sith_apprentice "Sith apprentice").[[165]](#cite_note-DB:Bane-165) Bane's Rule of Two was discovered by the Jedi,[[169]](#cite_note-Bane-SWE-169) but, as recounted by an imprint of later Jedi [Elzar Mann](/wiki/Elzar_Mann "Elzar Mann"), the Jedi Order believed they ended Bane's rule.[[170]](#cite_note-SW_2020_20-170) His death falsely convinced his enemies that the Sith had truly died out.[[169]](#cite_note-Bane-SWE-169)

### Keepers of the peace[]

#### Knights of the High Republic[]

##### Across the stars[]

:   "*I just didn't realize the Jedi ever had an official presence so far from the Core.*"  
    "*It's probably High Republic Era. It was a time of greatly expanded Jedi activity throughout the galaxy.*"
:   ―Luke Skywalker and Lor San Tekka[[75]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_2-75)

 [![The Jedi Order reached its zenith of power in the High Republic Era.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/be/LightAndLife-2021THR1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210107230623) [![The Jedi Order reached its zenith of power in the High Republic Era.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/be/LightAndLife-2021THR1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20210107230623)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/be/LightAndLife-2021THR1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210107230623) 

The Jedi Order reached its zenith of power in the High Republic Era.

 

The formation of the modern Galactic Republic heralded a new era of democracy, peace, and prosperity under the Galactic Senate and its elected leader, the Supreme Chancellor.[[125]](#cite_note-Propaganda-125) Due to the Galactic Republic's demilitarization, the Jedi Order fully embraced their responsibilities as peacekeepers and rejected their roles as soldiers. Assisted by the Republic [Judicials](/wiki/Judicial "Judicial"), the Jedi were responsible for maintaining law and order, namely by mediating conflicts to bring about peaceful solutions between various rival factions and planets,[[70]](#cite_note-Tarkin-70) as well as serving as interplanetary law enforcement by pursuing wanted and dangerous criminals, [pirates](/wiki/Pirate "Pirate"), and [smugglers](/wiki/Smuggler "Smuggler"). While they ultimately collapsed, the Galactic Republic and the Jedi Order were able to preside over a thousand years of peace sustained without major warfare.[[2]](#cite_note-UltimateSW-2) One of their philosophical sayings was "*the simplest gesture of kindness can fill a galaxy with hope.*"[[171]](#cite_note-Droids_in_Distress-171)

In approximately [319 BBY](/wiki/319_BBY "319 BBY"),[[172]](#cite_note-Aionomica_date-172) a copy of a third volume of the *Aionomica* was put forth. Though the existence of *Aionomicum III* had been rumored, this volume was later found to have been forged, causing a scandal.[[65]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-65) The Republic reached the zenith of its power and influence in a time remembered as the High Republic Era. During that time, the Republic relied heavily on the Jedi Order to render aid and settle disputes through peaceful methods.[[20]](#cite_note-TSWB-20) The Jedi worked alongside the Republic in its effort to expand into the [Outer Rim Territories](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Territories "Outer Rim Territories"), believing it also presented a chance to meet new groups and let them know they could rely on the Jedi for help. However, an [investigation](/wiki/Mission_to_Dalna_(Macri_and_Zink) "Mission to Dalna (Macri and Zink)") into the stolen [Rod of Seasons](/wiki/Rod_of_Seasons "Rod of Seasons") brought the Jedi into conflict with the Path of the Open Hand cult, which sought to use members of the [Nameless](/wiki/Shrikarai "Shrikarai") species against Force users in the name of "freeing" the Force.[[97]](#cite_note-Path_of_Deceit-97) The Jedi Order fought in[[129]](#cite_note-THR_2022_1-129) the [Republic-Togruta conflict](/wiki/Republic-Togruta_conflict "Republic-Togruta conflict").[[95]](#cite_note-The_Rising_Storm-95)

##### Defeating the Path[]

:   "*The Night of Sorrow is over, but the brave warriors who fell will not be forgotten. These Jedi came to answer our call of need without hesitation or doubt, because at the heart of the Jedi is a heart that fights for good. These Jedi fought bravely and selflessly, against the darkness that is ever-present in this galaxy.* […] *As stars are born and die, so does time move forward. Relentlessly so. And yet we fight. We will never stop fighting for the light and life in this galaxy.*"
:   ―Master Creighton Sun speaks after the Battle of Dalna[[114]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-114)

Padawan [Sav Malagán](/wiki/Savina_Besatrix_Malag%C3%A1n "Savina Besatrix Malagán") fought alongside [pirate queen](/wiki/Pirate_Queen "Pirate Queen") [Maz Kanata](/wiki/Maz_Kanata "Maz Kanata")'s crew during the [Battle of Jedha](/wiki/Battle_of_Jedha "Battle of Jedha"),[[173]](#cite_note-HRA_9-173) a conflict instigated by the Path. Several Jedi teams investigating the Path converged on Dalna, where the [Battle of Dalna](/wiki/Night_of_Sorrow "Night of Sorrow") exploded into being. The conflict had such a high death count it would devolve[[114]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-114) into massacre arguably caused by Republic and Jedi's close connection.[[174]](#cite_note-OOTS-174) All the same, much of the death was caused by the Path, which reformed into the war-like Path of the Closed Fist. During the battle, they also released Nameless that proved highly effective against the Jedi.[[114]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-114) Nonetheless, many [Dalnans](/wiki/Dalnan "Dalnan") held the Jedi responsible for the massacre they remembered as the "Night of Sorrow."[[175]](#cite_note-Mission_to_Disaster-175) At the time, however, the defeat of the Path was seen as proof of the benefits of Jedi-Republic partnership; as reasoned by former Supreme Chancellor [Kyong Greylark](/wiki/Kyong_Greylark "Kyong Greylark"), current Chancellor [Orlen Mollo](/wiki/Orlen_Mollo "Orlen Mollo"), and Master Yoda, the Path's defeat was only possible thanks to the work between both organizations, with their alliance a strength they believed the galaxy could call on for centuries to come.[[114]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-114)

After the battle, Yoda and Jedi Master [Creighton Sun](/wiki/Creighton_Sun "Creighton Sun") also agreed to cover up all information on the Nameless, including keep details on the creatures out of the Jedi Archives, until they learned more about the mysterious threat.[[114]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-114) However, one Jedi who encountered the effects of the Nameless,[[176]](#cite_note-Precedent-176) [Azlin Rell](/wiki/Azlin_Rell "Azlin Rell"), abandoned the Order and attempted to learn more about the creatures. Driven mad from his fear and falling to the dark side, Rell still heard the song [Shrii ka rai ka rai](/wiki/Shrii_ka_rai_ka_rai "Shrii ka rai ka rai")[[117]](#cite_note-Shadows_1-117) from his encounter with the Nameless on Dalna[[176]](#cite_note-Precedent-176) and kept the secrets he learned tucked away, yet still lost due to his insanity, in his mind.[[117]](#cite_note-Shadows_1-117)

##### Conflict with the Nihil[]

Even though some of its members would come to question whether it was right to do so, with Jedi like [Cohmac Vitus](/wiki/Cohmac_Vitus "Cohmac Vitus") remembering the massacre on Dalna as proof that the Republic and Jedi could not always act as one force,[[174]](#cite_note-OOTS-174) the Jedi continued to work closely with the Republic, with each organization respecting the strengths of the other. Thus, the Jedi aided the [Republic Defense Coalition](/wiki/Republic_Defense_Coalition "Republic Defense Coalition") and—through their outposts built to explore and help people in the wild portions of the Outer Rim—became the only group upholding justice in the Outer Rim Territories before the [dedication of the Starlight Beacon](/wiki/Dedication_of_the_Starlight_Beacon "Dedication of the Starlight Beacon"). During the era, the Order's understanding of the Force was expanded thanks to the actions of Jedi Knight [Elzar Mann](/wiki/Elzar_Mann "Elzar Mann"), who liked to "experiment" with his Force techniques in ways that sometimes failed. Even though he never attempted such actions when lives were at stake, his experiments often meant he worked alone.[[28]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-28)

Despite the High Republic's supposed peace, the Jedi were suddenly faced with a crisis during the [Great Hyperspace Disaster](/wiki/Great_Hyperspace_Disaster "Great Hyperspace Disaster") in the [Hetzal system](/wiki/Hetzal_system "Hetzal system") when the [transport](/wiki/Transport "Transport") *[Legacy Run](/wiki/Legacy_Run "Legacy Run")* was destroyed in hyperspace, making its remains rain upon the system. Jedi Master [Avar Kriss](/wiki/Avar_Kriss "Avar Kriss") commanded the rescue operation, yet she learned via her [Force bond](/wiki/Song_of_the_Force "Song of the Force") to the other Jedi that the fragments raining upon the Hetzal system contained living beings, forcing them to begin rescue operations as well. Towards the end of the crisis, the Jedi worked together—ultimately being joined in the Force by members of their Order who were even further away—to push a fragment containing liquid [Tibanna](/wiki/Tibanna "Tibanna") past the system's [R-class](/wiki/R-class "R-class") star. Their successful rescue of the system was broadcasted across the Outer Rim and even reached the Republic's inner planets. Unknown to the Jedi, the disaster had been masterminded by Eye of the [Nihil](/wiki/Nihil "Nihil"), Marchion Ro, who wanted revenge on the Jedi due to past events involving their Order, his [family](/wiki/Ro_family "Ro family"), and an [artifact](/wiki/Nameless_control_rods "Nameless control rods")[[28]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-28) that controlled a being known as the [Great Leveler](/wiki/Great_Leveler "Great Leveler"),[[95]](#cite_note-The_Rising_Storm-95) which was a member of the Nameless species[[177]](#cite_note-Trail_of_Shadows_5-177) and thus could overwhelm Jedi and other Force-sensitives.[[95]](#cite_note-The_Rising_Storm-95)

 [![The Nihil disrupted the peace of the High Republic Era by waging a conflict with the Jedi Order and the Galactic Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6a/LightOfTheJedi-OOPFullArt.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210112022621) [![The Nihil disrupted the peace of the High Republic Era by waging a conflict with the Jedi Order and the Galactic Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6a/LightOfTheJedi-OOPFullArt.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20210112022621)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6a/LightOfTheJedi-OOPFullArt.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210112022621) 

The Nihil disrupted the peace of the High Republic Era by waging a conflict with the Jedi Order and the Galactic Republic.

 

While Ro was not one to share details on what had exactly happened,[[95]](#cite_note-The_Rising_Storm-95) his ancestors, [Yana Ro](/wiki/Yana_Ro "Yana Ro") and [Marda Ro](/wiki/Marda_Ro "Marda Ro"), had been part of the Path,[[48]](#cite_note-Path_of_Vengeance-48) who were remembered as "the faithful" by later Ros. As the Ros later remembered, the Path fought the Jedi because of their differing opinions on "balance" and believed the Jedi were leading the galaxy towards its destruction. However, the Path was beaten back, with their religion mostly falling out of favor as time went by.[[95]](#cite_note-The_Rising_Storm-95) Inheriting the family goal of revenge and the title of "Eye" after his father [Asgar](/wiki/Asgar_Ro "Asgar Ro") was murdered, Ro plotted to reform the Nihil raiders into a unified force he could use for his ends and to beat back the expanding Republic. Additionally, the remains of the *Legacy Run* continued to rain upon Outer Rim systems as [Emergences](/wiki/Emergences "Emergences"), forcing the Republic to [blockade](/wiki/Blockade "Blockade") [hyperspace routes](/wiki/Hyperspace_route "Hyperspace route") and making the Jedi Council realize the Jedi would be needed in the Outer Rim more than normal. In time, the Order began to battle the Nihil, only for Ro to cement his control over the raiders after the [Battle of Kur](/wiki/Battle_of_Kur "Battle of Kur").[[28]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-28)

The Republic underestimated the Nihil until the massive [attack on Valo](/wiki/Valo_Atrocity "Valo Atrocity"), where the raiders cut down Jedi and civilian alike amid the [Valo Republic Fair](/wiki/Valo_Republic_Fair "Valo Republic Fair"), which was supposed to be Chancellor Soh's show of unity for the Republic. When the Jedi launched a counterattack through the [Battle of Grizal](/wiki/Battle_of_Grizal "Battle of Grizal"), Ro unleashed the Great Leveler, which petrified Jedi Master [Loden Greatstorm](/wiki/Loden_Greatstorm "Loden Greatstorm"),[[95]](#cite_note-The_Rising_Storm-95) leaving the Jedi to realize their enemy had a weapon they did not yet understand.[[178]](#cite_note-HRA_8-178) The Republic and Jedi Order grew closer during the Nihil conflict, with Soh and her aides even continually trying to become part of the Jedi High Council's meetings. As debate on how involved with the Republic they needed to become spread across the Order, many Jedi expressed worry that the Order's focus was at risk of moving to politics and war. Vitus was one such Jedi who questioned how much the Order actually owed the Republic, even though he agreed the Nihil were a serious threat, while his Padawan [Reath Silas](/wiki/Reath_Silas "Reath Silas") saw both sides to the debate.[[174]](#cite_note-OOTS-174)

 [![Starlight Beacon was destroyed during the conflict between the Jedi Order and the Nihil.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/23/THR-TheFallenStar-OOP-FullArt.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20220105191453) [![Starlight Beacon was destroyed during the conflict between the Jedi Order and the Nihil.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/23/THR-TheFallenStar-OOP-FullArt.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220105191453)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/23/THR-TheFallenStar-OOP-FullArt.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20220105191453) 

Starlight Beacon was destroyed during the conflict between the Jedi Order and the Nihil.

 

As the conflict and bloodshed carried on across the Galactic Frontier, more and more Jedi fell in battle against the Nihil, who the Jedi came to see were ruthless enemies who lacked any form of honor. Many Jedi had trouble adapting to the newly war-torn Outer Rim they needed to serve in. With it even coming to seem like acting only as peacekeepers was a recipe for defeat, Vitus came to believed the galaxy had grown to become a different place than the type the Jedi Order was made for and refused to finch in battle.[[96]](#cite_note-Midnight_Horizon-96) After Ro unleashed more Nameless during the [destruction of Starlight Beacon](/wiki/Destruction_of_Starlight_Beacon "Destruction of Starlight Beacon"), the Jedi Order's reputation took a hit when it ordered a mass recall of its members back to Coruscant; while Grand Master [Pra-Tre Veter](/wiki/Pra-Tre_Veter "Pra-Tre Veter") argued the Jedi needed to retreat until they could learn how to fight the Nameless, some Republic officials took it as the Jedi running away in fear.[[179]](#cite_note-Eye_2-179)

#### Beginning of the end[]

:   "*Do you think the Jedi will truly keep peace if they continue to take everything the Senate says as law?"  
    "Luckily, we are guided by our Council and not by politics nor ego.*"
:   ―[Dooku](/wiki/Dooku "Dooku") and [Mace Windu](/wiki/Mace_Windu "Mace Windu")[[131]](#cite_note-Choices-131)

 [![Premonitions of a galactic conflict caused Jedi Master Sifo-Dyas to commission the creation of a clone army.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1e/Sifo-Dyas-TCWCEJtB.png/revision/latest?cb=20241216040719) [![Premonitions of a galactic conflict caused Jedi Master Sifo-Dyas to commission the creation of a clone army.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1e/Sifo-Dyas-TCWCEJtB.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20241216040719)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1e/Sifo-Dyas-TCWCEJtB.png/revision/latest?cb=20241216040719) 

Premonitions of a galactic conflict caused Jedi Master Sifo-Dyas to commission the creation of a clone army.

 

Prior to the [Invasion of Naboo](/wiki/Invasion_of_Naboo "Invasion of Naboo"), Jedi Master [Sifo-Dyas](/wiki/Sifo-Dyas "Sifo-Dyas") served on the Jedi High Council until he was removed from its ranks for advocating the mobilization of a Republic Military to defend the galaxy.[[180]](#cite_note-Sifo-Dyas_DB-180) Through the Force, Sifo-Dyas predicted a galactic conflict but the High Council at the time considered his views radical.[[181]](#cite_note-The_Lost_One-181) Certain in the accuracy of his [Force visions](/wiki/Force_vision "Force vision"), Sifo-Dyas secretly commissioned the inhabitants of [Kamino](/wiki/Kamino "Kamino") to [grow](/wiki/Bioengineering "Bioengineering") an army of clone soldiers[[180]](#cite_note-Sifo-Dyas_DB-180)—[genetically engineered](/wiki/Bioengineering "Bioengineering") for growth acceleration and increased docility[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_II-8)—for the Republic. Unbeknownst to Sifo-Dyas, however, his plan factored into the designs of the Sith.[[180]](#cite_note-Sifo-Dyas_DB-180) For a [millennium](/wiki/Millennium "Millennium"), generations of [Sith Lords](/wiki/Sith_Lord "Sith Lord") plotted revenge against the Jedi Order after the death of [Darth](/wiki/Darth "Darth") Bane. Darth Sidious, who had become a Sith Master after betraying and murdering his master [Darth Plagueis](/wiki/Darth_Plagueis "Darth Plagueis"), was the culmination of the [Grand Plan](/wiki/Grand_Plan "Grand Plan") that would see the Sith returned to a position of dominance over the galaxy.[[169]](#cite_note-Bane-SWE-169)

After serving as an unwitting pawn for the Sith, Sifo-Dyas was betrayed by his childhood friend,[[9]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost-9) the Jedi Master [Count](/wiki/Count "Count") Dooku, who had him [assassinated](/wiki/Mission_to_Felucia_(Sifo-Dyas) "Mission to Felucia (Sifo-Dyas)") by the [Pyke Syndicate](/wiki/Pyke_Syndicate "Pyke Syndicate") at the behest of Sidious.[[180]](#cite_note-Sifo-Dyas_DB-180) Disillusioned with the Jedi Order, yet also ambitious for power, Dooku rejected the light side and became a Sith Lord, adopting the moniker of Darth Tyranus,[[182]](#cite_note-Dooku_DB-182) and replacing [Darth Maul](/wiki/Maul "Maul") as the Sith apprentice of Darth Sidious.[[183]](#cite_note-The_Lawless-183)

 [![From the shadows, the Sith controlled the creation of the clone army.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/18/JangoFettMeetsWithDooku-AORJangoFett1.png/revision/latest?cb=20190111035238) [![From the shadows, the Sith controlled the creation of the clone army.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/18/JangoFettMeetsWithDooku-AORJangoFett1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20190111035238)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/18/JangoFettMeetsWithDooku-AORJangoFett1.png/revision/latest?cb=20190111035238) 

From the shadows, the Sith controlled the creation of the clone army.

 

The Sith guided the creation of the clone [troopers](/wiki/Trooper "Trooper") after Sifo-Dyas' death, covertly taking control of the army[[180]](#cite_note-Sifo-Dyas_DB-180) and its [Kaminoan](/wiki/Kaminoan "Kaminoan") developers. Tyranus maintained secret contact with two officials of the [Kaminoan government](/wiki/Ruling_Council_(Kamino) "Ruling Council (Kamino)"), [Prime Minister](/wiki/Prime_Minister "Prime Minister") [Lama Su](/wiki/Lama_Su "Lama Su") and the [Chief Medical Scientist](/wiki/Chief_Medical_Scientist "Chief Medical Scientist") [Doctor](/wiki/Doctor "Doctor") [Nala Se](/wiki/Nala_Se "Nala Se"), who were supplied with [behavioral modification biochips](/wiki/Behavioral_modification_biochip "Behavioral modification biochip") to ensure the clones' compliance with their[[184]](#cite_note-Conspiracy-184) Sith programming.[[185]](#cite_note-The_Unknown-185) The chips were implanted in the [brain](/wiki/Brain "Brain") of every clone trooper during the early stage of their development;[[186]](#cite_note-Fugitive-186) Sifo-Dyas, who originally thought of the chip, intended for it to be a safeguard against rogue Jedi, but Tyranus and Sidious retooled the chip. Tyranus deceived the Kaminoans into believing Sifo-Dyas' intention.[[184]](#cite_note-Conspiracy-184) However, the biochip's true purpose was to guarantee that the clones would carry out Order 66,[[187]](#cite_note-Orders-187) a [secret protocol](/wiki/Executive_Order_Codes_for_the_Grand_Army_of_the_Republic "Executive Order Codes for the Grand Army of the Republic")[[186]](#cite_note-Fugitive-186) that was integral to the destruction of the Jedi Order.[[188]](#cite_note-Shattered-188)

### Invasion of Naboo[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Invasion of Naboo](/wiki/Invasion_of_Naboo "Invasion of Naboo")

:   "*At last we will reveal ourselves to the Jedi. At last we will have revenge.*"
:   ―Darth Maul, to Darth Sidious — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6b/RevengeAtLast-TPM.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250307223813)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:RevengeAtLast-TPM.flac "File:RevengeAtLast-TPM.flac"))[[25]](#cite_note-Episode_I-25)

 [![Anakin Skywalker was the Chosen One discovered by the Jedi in the late Republic Era.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6a/NiceToMeetYouFutureMassMurderer-TPM.png/revision/latest?cb=20200915083929) [![Anakin Skywalker was the Chosen One discovered by the Jedi in the late Republic Era.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6a/NiceToMeetYouFutureMassMurderer-TPM.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200915083929)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6a/NiceToMeetYouFutureMassMurderer-TPM.png/revision/latest?cb=20200915083929) 

Anakin Skywalker was the Chosen One discovered by the Jedi in the late Republic Era.

 

In [32 BBY](/wiki/32_BBY "32 BBY"),[[40]](#cite_note-Galactic_Atlas-40) Supreme Chancellor [Finis Valorum](/wiki/Finis_Valorum "Finis Valorum") requested the Jedi Order's assistance in negotiating a dispute that resulted in the [Trade Federation](/wiki/Trade_Federation "Trade Federation")'s [blockade](/wiki/Blockade "Blockade") of the planet [Naboo](/wiki/Naboo "Naboo"). The High Council dispatched Jedi Master [Qui-Gon Jinn](/wiki/Qui-Gon_Jinn "Qui-Gon Jinn") and his Padawan, Obi-Wan Kenobi, to negotiate with the Trade Federation. However, Darth Sidious, whose public persona was [Senator](/wiki/Senator "Senator") Sheev Palpatine of Naboo, insisted that the Trade Federation, which was under his sway, initiated an invasion of Naboo and overwhelmed the [Royal Naboo Security Forces](/wiki/Royal_Naboo_Security_Forces "Royal Naboo Security Forces"). Circumventing a trap by the Federation, Jinn and Kenobi were able to escape to Naboo and arrive in [Theed](/wiki/Theed "Theed") in time to rescue the [Naboo](/wiki/Royal_House_of_Naboo "Royal House of Naboo") [Queen](/wiki/Queen "Queen"), [Padmé Amidala](/wiki/Padm%C3%A9_Amidala "Padmé Amidala"), who was being held captive by Federation forces. Together with the Queen's [Handmaidens](/wiki/Naboo_Royal_Handmaidens "Naboo Royal Handmaidens") and her close [security detail](/wiki/Naboo_Palace_Guard "Naboo Palace Guard"), the Jedi fled the planet but their [ship](/wiki/Starship "Starship") was damaged in the escape, causing them to land on the desert planet of [Tatooine](/wiki/Tatooine "Tatooine").[[25]](#cite_note-Episode_I-25)

 [![After a thousand years in hiding, the Sith revealed themselves to the Jedi during the Invasion of Naboo.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/08/DotF_TPM.png/revision/latest?cb=20240522042217) [![After a thousand years in hiding, the Sith revealed themselves to the Jedi during the Invasion of Naboo.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/08/DotF_TPM.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20240522042217)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/08/DotF_TPM.png/revision/latest?cb=20240522042217) 

After a thousand years in hiding, the Sith revealed themselves to the Jedi during the Invasion of Naboo.

 

While stranded on Tatooine, the two Jedi discovered a young slave named [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker"). Jinn believed Anakin to be the Chosen One, the one that would bring balance to the Force. By betting on the boy winning the [Boonta Eve Classic](/wiki/Boonta_Eve_Classic "Boonta Eve Classic"), Jinn was able to secure both Skywalker's freedom and the needed parts to repair the [Queen's ship](/wiki/Naboo_Royal_Starship "Naboo Royal Starship") to reach Coruscant. It was after this that Jinn was [attacked](/wiki/Duel_on_Tatooine "Duel on Tatooine") by Darth Maul, apprentice to Darth Sidious, who had dispatched Maul to kill the Jedi. As the Jedi had believed the Sith to be extinct, Jinn was at first unsure of who Maul was except that he had been trained in lightsaber combat. Arriving at the Jedi Temple on Coruscant, the Council refused to induct Skywalker into the Order because, according to the the Code, he was too old. The Council then ordered Jinn and Kenobi to protect Queen Amidala on her return to Theed. At the same time, Amidala was deceived by Palpatine into calling for a [Vote of No Confidence](/wiki/Vote_of_No_Confidence "Vote of No Confidence") in Chancellor Valorum, which would eventually lead to the election of Palpatine to the chancellorship. Jinn and Kenobi then assisted Amidala and her forces during the ensuing [battle](/wiki/Battle_of_Naboo "Battle of Naboo") against the Trade Federation, when Maul killed Jinn in [combat](/wiki/Lightsaber_combat "Lightsaber combat"), only for the Sith to be defeated by Kenobi. Given the status of Jedi Knight afterward, Kenobi took Skywalker as his apprentice, despite Yoda's reluctance,[[25]](#cite_note-Episode_I-25) and the Jedi Order was left in the dark as to what the Sith's actions were for ten years.[[40]](#cite_note-Galactic_Atlas-40)[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_II-8) The Jedi were left unaware that they were being deceived by Palpatine, who was using his double identity to eventually complete the Sith's revenge by destroying the Jedi and taking over the Republic.[[19]](#cite_note-Episode_III-19)

### Separatist Crisis[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Separatist Crisis](/wiki/Separatist_Crisis "Separatist Crisis")

:   "*I will not let this Republic that has stood for a thousand years be split in two. My negotiations will not fail.*"  
    "*If they do, you must realize that there aren't enough Jedi to protect the Republic. We're keepers of the peace, not soldiers.*"
:   ―Sheev Palpatine and Mace Windu[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_II-8)

 [![The Separatist Crisis threatened to end the era of peace established by the Republic and the Jedi.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6e/Chancellors_Office.png/revision/latest?cb=20161015185023) [![The Separatist Crisis threatened to end the era of peace established by the Republic and the Jedi.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6e/Chancellors_Office.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161015185023)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6e/Chancellors_Office.png/revision/latest?cb=20161015185023) 

The Separatist Crisis threatened to end the era of peace established by the Republic and the Jedi.

 

Having broken all ties to the Jedi Order, secretly replacing Maul as Sidious' apprentice, Dooku was believed to be a mere "political idealist" by his peers at the Jedi Order.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_II-8) For eight years, Dooku was scarcely heard about until he staged a theatrical return to public life by delivering a rousing speech that condemned the Republic and essentially set the stage for the [Separatist Crisis](/wiki/Separatist_Crisis "Separatist Crisis"). At the same time, he fomented political turmoil in many worlds, including Ryloth, [Kashyyyk](/wiki/Kashyyyk "Kashyyyk"), [Sullust](/wiki/Sullust "Sullust"), and Onderon, or tried to convince their leaders to leave the Republic, as in [Eriadu](/wiki/Eriadu "Eriadu")'s case.[[70]](#cite_note-Tarkin-70) Soon enough, Dooku became the face of the Confederacy of Independent Systems, convincing several thousand systems to leave the Republic.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_II-8)

 [![Jedi Knight Obi-Wan Kenobi journeyed to Kamino where he discovered the creation of a clone army.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/dc/Kenobi-Visits-Kamino.png/revision/latest?cb=20210516171856) [![Jedi Knight Obi-Wan Kenobi journeyed to Kamino where he discovered the creation of a clone army.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/dc/Kenobi-Visits-Kamino.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20210516171856)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/dc/Kenobi-Visits-Kamino.png/revision/latest?cb=20210516171856) 

Jedi Knight Obi-Wan Kenobi journeyed to Kamino where he discovered the creation of a clone army.

 

The Jedi Order was unable to ensure the Republic's safety in the event of a war due to its limited numbers. The Republic lacked a standing army, while the mandate of the Jedi was to maintain order as peacekeepers instead of soldiers. Concerned by the growing number of star systems seceding from the Republic, the Senate debated the [Military Creation Act](/wiki/Military_Creation_Act "Military Creation Act"). During the debate, a [plot to assassinate Senator Amidala](/wiki/Plot_to_assassinate_Senator_Amidala "Plot to assassinate Senator Amidala") forced the Naboo senator to return to her homeworld with Padawan Anakin Skywalker serving as her [bodyguard](/wiki/Bodyguard "Bodyguard"). The task of investigating the plot against Amidala was given to Skywalker's master, Jedi Knight Obi-Wan Kenobi, who [tracked](/wiki/Mission_to_Kamino_(Separatist_Crisis) "Mission to Kamino (Separatist Crisis)") the [assassin](/wiki/Assassin "Assassin") to the planet Kamino.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_II-8)

After discovering the Kaminoans' creation of the clone army at the behest of the late Jedi Master Sifo-Dyas, Kenobi deduced that the army's clone template, the [bounty hunter](/wiki/Bounty_hunter "Bounty hunter") [Jango Fett](/wiki/Jango_Fett "Jango Fett"), was the assassin who tried to kill Amidala. Jango and his cloned son, [Boba Fett](/wiki/Boba_Fett "Boba Fett"), fled from Kamino to escape interrogation by the Jedi. However, Kenobi [followed](/wiki/Dogfight_over_Geonosis "Dogfight over Geonosis") the [Fetts](/wiki/Fetts "Fetts") to [Geonosis](/wiki/Geonosis "Geonosis") where he discovered the [Separatist Droid Army](/wiki/Separatist_Droid_Army "Separatist Droid Army"), prompting the Senate to empower Chancellor Palpatine to unilaterally create the Grand Army of the Republic.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_II-8)

### Clone Wars[]

#### The first battle[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars")

:   "*I have to admit that without the clones, it would not have been a victory.*"  
    "*Victory? Victory, you say? Master Obi-Wan, not victory. The shroud of the dark side has fallen. Begun the Clone War has.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi and Yoda[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_II-8)

As the Republic prepared for war, Jedi Master Mace Windu led a [Jedi assault team](/wiki/Jedi_assault_team "Jedi assault team") to rescue Kenobi on Geonosis. The Jedi confronted the Separatists in the [Geonosian](/wiki/Geonosian "Geonosian") [Petranaki Arena](/wiki/Petranaki_Arena "Petranaki Arena"), destroying many [battle droids](/wiki/Battle_droid "Battle droid") but also sustaining a large number of casualties,[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_II-8) including [Tan Yuster](/wiki/Tan_Yuster "Tan Yuster"),[[189]](#cite_note-Lightsabers-189) [Sar Labooda](/wiki/Sar_Labooda "Sar Labooda"),[[2]](#cite_note-UltimateSW-2) and [Coleman Trebor](/wiki/Coleman_Trebor "Coleman Trebor"). The remaining Jedi were evacuated from the arena by the Republic clone army that arrived on Geonosis under the command of Grand Master Yoda.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_II-8)

 [![Through the combined efforts of Jedi and clones, the Republic defeated the Separatists in the first battle of the Clone Wars.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/46/Clone_Army_Charge.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160125191812) [![Through the combined efforts of Jedi and clones, the Republic defeated the Separatists in the first battle of the Clone Wars.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/46/Clone_Army_Charge.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160125191812)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/46/Clone_Army_Charge.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160125191812) 

Through the combined efforts of Jedi and clones, the Republic defeated the Separatists in the first battle of the Clone Wars.

 

Along with the requisite [LAAT](/wiki/Low_Altitude_Assault_Transport "Low Altitude Assault Transport") [gunships](/wiki/Gunship "Gunship") and [AT-TE](/wiki/All_Terrain_Tactical_Enforcer "All Terrain Tactical Enforcer") [walkers](/wiki/Walker "Walker"), over eighty [regiments](/wiki/Regiment "Regiment") of clone troopers[[6]](#cite_note-CL_2016-6) engaged the droid army with the Jedi leading the charge.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_II-8) Although the Jedi had not yet received a formal commission in the newly formed Grand Army,[[6]](#cite_note-CL_2016-6) the clones nonetheless complied with their orders. Windu, [Kit Fisto](/wiki/Kit_Fisto "Kit Fisto"), [Aayla Secura](/wiki/Aayla_Secura "Aayla Secura"), and other Jedi fought alongside their [troops](/wiki/Troop "Troop") on the battlefield while Yoda was occupied with overseeing the Republic army's strategy from the [forward command center](/wiki/Forward_Command_Center "Forward Command Center"). The Republic attack caught the Separatist leaders by surprise; despite their initial efforts to organize an effective counterattack, the Separatists ultimately retreated from Geonosis[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_II-8) as the clones achieved ground and air supremacy under the skilled leadership of the Jedi High Council.[[6]](#cite_note-CL_2016-6) Although the [First Battle of Geonosis](/wiki/First_Battle_of_Geonosis "First Battle of Geonosis") concluded as a victory for the Republic, Yoda lamented its outcome as the beginning of the Clone Wars.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_II-8) The outbreak of the conflict alone was enough to shift the Force's balance.[[190]](#cite_note-Battle_of_GeoTrailer-190)

#### Jedi of the Republic[]

:   "*We do what we have trained our whole lives to do. Trust in the Force. Believe in the path that is set out before us. Stand in defense of all peoples, not just of the Republic, but across the galaxy. We do what any Jedi would when staring into the face of evil. We fight.*"
:   ―Mace Windu[[141]](#cite_note-Mace_Windu_5-141)

 [![The advent of the Clone Wars forced the Jedi to lead the Grand Army of the Republic and Republic Navy.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/97/Ahsoka8-BigTimetextless.png/revision/latest?cb=20250204204858) [![The advent of the Clone Wars forced the Jedi to lead the Grand Army of the Republic and Republic Navy.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/97/Ahsoka8-BigTimetextless.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250204204858)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/97/Ahsoka8-BigTimetextless.png/revision/latest?cb=20250204204858) 

The advent of the Clone Wars forced the Jedi to lead the Grand Army of the Republic and Republic Navy.

 

The aftermath of the battle on Geonosis saw the Jedi commissioned as [officers](/wiki/Officer "Officer") of the Republic Military, with the [military rank](/wiki/Military_rank "Military rank") of Jedi General bestowed to Knights and Masters,[[191]](#cite_note-Mace_Windu_1-191) and the rank of [Jedi Commander](/wiki/Jedi_Commander "Jedi Commander") to Padawans.[[55]](#cite_note-TCWFilm-55) The [Jedi Military Integration Act](/wiki/Jedi_Military_Integration_Act "Jedi Military Integration Act") formallized this and offically made the Jedi Order a part of the Republic Military.[[192]](#cite_note-Brotherhood-192) The Jedi were not of a single mind regarding participation in the war. Some Jedi felt they have lost something by becoming the Republic's warriors, but, on the other hand, other Jedi believed that returning to monasticism and contemplation would mean ignoring the suffering going on in the galaxy.[[193]](#cite_note-Collapse-193) Mace Windu believed that the Jedi should strive to serve as an example by leading the Republic's soldiers on the battlefield, although he was nonetheless affected by the loss of Jedi lives early in the conflict. Windu was troubled by the prospect of more Jedi dying as a result of the Order's decision to fight in the Clone Wars, but Yoda counseled his colleague to set aside his doubts and trust in the Force, acknowledging Windu for his wisdom and capable leadership.[[191]](#cite_note-Mace_Windu_1-191)

Jedi Master [Prosset Dibs](/wiki/Tenth_Brother "Tenth Brother"), meanwhile, opposed Jedi involvement in the war and disliked needing to be involved in battle at all. While still able to fight as a skilled warrior, he felt the Force shudder due to the conflict and remained steadfast in his belief that war was no place for a Jedi.[[191]](#cite_note-Mace_Windu_1-191) Dibs and Windu's opposing views came to a head during a [mission to counter Separatist operations](/wiki/Operation_on_Hissrich "Operation on Hissrich") on the planet [Hissrich](/wiki/Hissrich "Hissrich"), where Dibs was horrified by the civilian cost of war and came to believe the High Council was more interested in the world's resources than protecting its people. Dibs attacked Windu[[194]](#cite_note-Mace_Windu_3-194) but was ultimately defeated, with the master standing trial before the High Council after the mission. However, Windu called on the High Council to grant clemency to Dibs, who had stood by his actions and wanted to be put to death to prove that the High Council were nothing more than warmongers. Despite his personal reservations, Windu's experience on Hissrich reminded him of the Jedi Order's commitment to safeguarding the lives of others. With his newfound resolve, Windu affirmed his belief that the Order had a moral responsibility to defend the citizens of the Republic as well as all beings throughout the galaxy.[[141]](#cite_note-Mace_Windu_5-141)

During the Clone Wars, the Jedi were victorious on battlefronts across the galaxy, including [Christophsis](/wiki/Christophsis "Christophsis"),[[55]](#cite_note-TCWFilm-55) Ryloth,[[150]](#cite_note-Liberty_on_Ryloth-150) and [Umbara](/wiki/Umbara "Umbara").[[195]](#cite_note-CoK-195) In their capacity as leaders of the Grand Army of the Republic, the Jedi came to be seen as great warriors. Jedi Knight Anakin Skywalker, for example, was considered by some to be the greatest warrior of the Jedi Order[[36]](#cite_note-Shroud_of_Darkness-36) and became known as the "[Hero With No Fear](/wiki/Hero_With_No_Fear "Hero With No Fear")" to the [HoloNet](/wiki/HoloNet "HoloNet").[[192]](#cite_note-Brotherhood-192) Believing the Order was not political, one Separatist fighter, [Poan of Riek](/wiki/Poan_of_Riek "Poan of Riek"), believed the war would end quickly because he thought the Jedi would, soon enough, intervene against the Republic. However, Poan then came face-to-face against a Jedi during a [Mission on Leyoye Prime](/wiki/Mission_on_Leyoye_Prime "Mission on Leyoye Prime"), in which the Jedi singlehandedly wiped out most of his unit.[[196]](#cite_note-MoF-196)

 [![The Battle of Christophsis was an early victory for the Jedi-led forces of the Galactic Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5d/Christophsismeeting.png/revision/latest?cb=20121013042053) [![The Battle of Christophsis was an early victory for the Jedi-led forces of the Galactic Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5d/Christophsismeeting.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20121013042053)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5d/Christophsismeeting.png/revision/latest?cb=20121013042053) 

The Battle of Christophsis was an early victory for the Jedi-led forces of the Galactic Republic.

 

During the [Battle of Christophsis](/wiki/Battle_of_Christophsis "Battle of Christophsis"), [Clone Sergeant](/wiki/Clone_Sergeant "Clone Sergeant") [Slick](/wiki/Slick "Slick") was arrested as a [spy](/wiki/Spy "Spy") for the Confederacy of Independent Systems. The [sergeant](/wiki/Sergeant "Sergeant") claimed that he acted in the interests of the clones, whom he viewed as a slave army fighting for the Jedi and the Republic. However, the [clone trooper officers](/wiki/Clone_trooper_officer "Clone trooper officer") who arrested him—[Clone Commander](/wiki/Clone_Commander "Clone Commander") [Cody](/wiki/Cody "Cody") and [Clone Captain](/wiki/Clone_Captain "Clone Captain") [Rex](/wiki/Rex "Rex")—questioned Slick's motives, noting how he betrayed the Republic for money and that his actions endangered clone lives. Although Slick succeeded in sabotaging much of the Republic's military equipment,[[197]](#cite_note-The_Hidden_Enemy-197) Jedi Generals Obi-Wan Kenobi and Anakin Skywalker successfully led their [battalions](/wiki/Battalion "Battalion"), respectively the [212th Attack Battalion](/wiki/212th_Attack_Battalion "212th Attack Battalion") and the [501st Legion](/wiki/501st_Legion "501st Legion"), to victory over the Separatists on the [Christophsian](/wiki/Christophsian "Christophsian") homeworld.[[55]](#cite_note-TCWFilm-55)

 [![The Jedi's forces won the Battle of Ryloth with the support of the Twi'lek Resistance.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/02/Triumphant_fighters_on_Ryloth.png/revision/latest?cb=20121005170920) [![The Jedi's forces won the Battle of Ryloth with the support of the Twi'lek Resistance.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/02/Triumphant_fighters_on_Ryloth.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20121005170920)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/02/Triumphant_fighters_on_Ryloth.png/revision/latest?cb=20121005170920) 

The Jedi's forces won the Battle of Ryloth with the support of the Twi'lek Resistance.

 

The Battle of Ryloth was a coordinated effort by the Republic to liberate the Twi'leks' homeworld from Separatist occupation. With the Jedi in command, the clone troopers mainly relied on using [blaster rifles](/wiki/Blaster_rifle "Blaster rifle") and [Electro Magnetic Pulse grenades](/wiki/Electromagnetic_pulse_grenade "Electromagnetic pulse grenade") to reduce the level of destruction on Ryloth. Whereas the Separatists used the Twi'leks as living shields to deter a direct Republic attack, the Jedi and their clones were careful to avoid causing civilian casualties.[[198]](#cite_note-Innocents_of_Ryloth-198) During the final phase of the invasion, General Windu endeavored to take the capital city of [Lessu](/wiki/Lessu_City "Lessu City") with the support of the Twi'lek Resistance led by Cham Syndulla.[[150]](#cite_note-Liberty_on_Ryloth-150) Setting aside his dislike for politics,[[20]](#cite_note-TSWB-20) Windu used diplomacy to win the freedom fighter's help, convincing the rivals Syndulla and Senator [Orn Free Taa](/wiki/Orn_Free_Taa "Orn Free Taa") to work together in common cause. The combined forces of Jedi, Republic, and Twi-leks captured the capital along with the Separatist [Emir of Ryloth](/wiki/Emir_of_Ryloth "Emir of Ryloth") [Wat Tambor](/wiki/Wat_Tambor "Wat Tambor").[[150]](#cite_note-Liberty_on_Ryloth-150)

 [![The Jedi successfully invaded Geonosis and destroyed the primary battle droid foundry.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/da/SecondGeonosis.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20101226090521) [![The Jedi successfully invaded Geonosis and destroyed the primary battle droid foundry.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/da/SecondGeonosis.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20101226090521)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/da/SecondGeonosis.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20101226090521) 

The Jedi successfully invaded Geonosis and destroyed the primary battle droid foundry.

 

The [Second Battle of Geonosis](/wiki/Second_Battle_of_Geonosis "Second Battle of Geonosis") occurred after the Geonosian resistance ousted the Republic's [occupation force](/wiki/Occupation_of_Geonosis "Occupation of Geonosis") from their world. With the Separatists in control of the [Geonosian droid factories](/wiki/Geonosis_droid_factories "Geonosis droid factories") once more, the Jedi returned to Geonosis at the head of an invasion force, having deemed Geonosis crucial to their efforts at restoring order to the Republic. The attack was led by Jedi Generals [Ki-Adi-Mundi](/wiki/Ki-Adi-Mundi "Ki-Adi-Mundi"), Obi-Wan Kenobi, [Luminara Unduli](/wiki/Luminara_Unduli "Luminara Unduli"), and Anakin Skywalker.[[199]](#cite_note-Landing_at_Point_Rain-199) After the generals' forces converged at the [Point Rain](/wiki/Point_Rain "Point Rain") [staging area](/wiki/Staging_area "Staging area"), the [primary droid foundry](/wiki/Geonosis_primary_droid_foundry "Geonosis primary droid foundry") was destroyed by Jedi [Commanders](/wiki/Commander "Commander") [Barriss Offee](/wiki/Barriss_Offee "Barriss Offee") and [Ahsoka Tano](/wiki/Ahsoka_Tano "Ahsoka Tano").[[200]](#cite_note-Weapons_Factory-200) The capture of [Archduke](/wiki/Archduke "Archduke") [Poggle the Lesser](/wiki/Poggle_the_Lesser "Poggle the Lesser") subsequently ended Separatist control of Geonosis,[[201]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Terror-201) thereby depriving the Confederacy military of further support against the Republic from Geonosis.[[202]](#cite_note-DB_Geo-202)

#### Rogue Jedi[]

:   "*I did it because I've come to realize what many people in the Republic have come to realize, that the Jedi are the ones responsible for this war, that we've so lost our way that we have become villains in this conflict, that we are the ones that should be put on trial, all of us! And my attack on the Temple was an attack on what the Jedi have become, an army fighting for the dark side, fallen from the light that we once held so dear. This Republic is failing! It's only a matter of time.*"
:   ―Barriss Offee, admitting to the bombing of the Jedi Temple hangar[[56]](#cite_note-TWJ-56)

By the time of the [Alderaan Refugee Conference](/wiki/Alderaan_Refugee_Conference "Alderaan Refugee Conference"), Padmé Amidala stated that over one hundred Jedi had been killed in the war.[[203]](#cite_note-Assassin-203) More Jedi were killed as the war continued; Jedi Master [Even Piell](/wiki/Even_Piell "Even Piell") died at the [Battle of Lola Sayu](/wiki/Battle_of_Lola_Sayu "Battle of Lola Sayu");[[204]](#cite_note-Citadel_Rescue-204) during the [assault](/wiki/Assault_on_Vizsla_Keep_09 "Assault on Vizsla Keep 09") on [Vizsla Keep 09](/wiki/Vizsla_Keep_09 "Vizsla Keep 09"), Count Dooku killed Jedi Master [Tiplee](/wiki/Tiplee "Tiplee").[[205]](#cite_note-DM:SoD-205) In addition to the casualties of war, the Jedi Order lost a few of its members to the dark side of the Force, such as Jedi Master [Pong Krell](/wiki/Pong_Krell "Pong Krell")[[195]](#cite_note-CoK-195) and Padawan Barriss Offee.[[56]](#cite_note-TWJ-56)

 [![Jedi General Pong Krell assumed command of the 501st Legion during the Battle of Umbara.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/91/Epguide408.png/revision/latest?cb=20121126050322) [![Jedi General Pong Krell assumed command of the 501st Legion during the Battle of Umbara.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/91/Epguide408.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20121126050322)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/91/Epguide408.png/revision/latest?cb=20121126050322) 

Jedi General Pong Krell assumed command of the 501st Legion during the Battle of Umbara.

 

Krell served in the Clone Wars as a successful Jedi General whose record reflected numerous victories for the Grand Army of the Republic.[[206]](#cite_note-Pong_Krell_DB-206) His command style resulted in high levels of clone trooper casualties; nevertheless, Krell was an acclaimed war hero by the time of the [Battle of Umbara](/wiki/Battle_of_Umbara "Battle of Umbara"),[[207]](#cite_note-The_General-207) during which he temporarily assumed command of the 501st [Legion](/wiki/Legion "Legion") after Anakin Skywalker returned to Coruscant at the behest of the Jedi High Council and Chancellor Palpatine.[[208]](#cite_note-Darkness_Umbara-208)
