Though originally a Republic [loyalist](/wiki/Loyalist "Loyalist") world at the onset of the Clone Wars,[[3]](#cite_note-Rise_of_the_Separatists-3) Umbara defected to the Separatists in the wake of Senator [Mee Deechi](/wiki/Mee_Deechi "Mee Deechi")'s assassination. The Republic therefore invaded the [Umbaran](/wiki/Umbaran "Umbaran") homeworld, precipitating the Battle of Umbara.[[208]](#cite_note-Darkness_Umbara-208) By then, Krell had foreseen the rise of a [New Order](/wiki/New_Order "New Order") in the aftermath of the Clone Wars. Convinced that the Jedi Order would be defeated, Krell secretly turned against both the Order and the Republic. He sought to prove his new loyalties to Count Dooku by undermining the Republic's efforts to retake Umbara. However, Krell's plans ended when the 501st mutinied against the general's command. Krell was taken into custody after killing multiple clones while resisting arrest. Ultimately, the fallen Jedi Master was executed by[[195]](#cite_note-CoK-195) one of his strongest supporters, [Dogma](/wiki/Dogma "Dogma"),[[209]](#cite_note-Dogma_DB-209) after admitting his betrayal of the Republic.[[195]](#cite_note-CoK-195)

 [![Barriss Offee was arrested for perpetrating of an attack on the Jedi Temple and conspiring to incriminate Ahsoka Tano.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a0/BarrissInCourt-TWJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20131029031520) [![Barriss Offee was arrested for perpetrating of an attack on the Jedi Temple and conspiring to incriminate Ahsoka Tano.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a0/BarrissInCourt-TWJ.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20131029031520)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a0/BarrissInCourt-TWJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20131029031520) 

Barriss Offee was arrested for perpetrating of an attack on the Jedi Temple and conspiring to incriminate Ahsoka Tano.

 

Barriss Offee believed the Jedi had deviated from their course as peacekeepers and so arranged a [bombing](/wiki/Bombing_of_the_Jedi_Temple_hangar "Bombing of the Jedi Temple hangar") at the Jedi Temple, for which framed fellow Padawan Ahsoka Tano. Tano, in turn, left the Jedi Order unable to trust the Council after turning its back on her during her [trial](/wiki/Trial_of_Ahsoka_Tano "Trial of Ahsoka Tano").[[56]](#cite_note-TWJ-56) Eventually, the High Council came to be aware of Dooku's hand in the creation of the clone army, and of the lies and mistrust that surrounded them, both inside the Temple and the Senate.[[210]](#cite_note-Voices-210) Grand Master Yoda even (as it turned out correctly) foresaw that the Jedi might not win the Clone Wars,[[158]](#cite_note-Sacrifice-158) just as public support for the Jedi weakened due to their management of the conflict.[[69]](#cite_note-Sabotage-69)

#### The last stand[]

:   "*In the name of the Galactic Senate of the Republic, you're under arrest, Chancellor.*"  
    "*Are you threatening me, Master Jedi?*"  
    "*The Senate will decide your fate.*"
:   ―Mace Windu and Sheev Palpatine[[19]](#cite_note-Episode_III-19)

 [![The High Council moved to arrest Supreme Chancellor Sheev Palpatine, revealed to be the Sith Lord Darth Sidious.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b9/DuelonCoruscant.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111028234030) [![The High Council moved to arrest Supreme Chancellor Sheev Palpatine, revealed to be the Sith Lord Darth Sidious.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b9/DuelonCoruscant.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20111028234030)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b9/DuelonCoruscant.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111028234030) 

The High Council moved to arrest Supreme Chancellor Sheev Palpatine, revealed to be the Sith Lord Darth Sidious.

 

The war would come to an end in [19 BBY](/wiki/19_BBY "19 BBY")[[40]](#cite_note-Galactic_Atlas-40) after Sidious betrayed and orchestrated Tyranus' death in the [Battle of Coruscant](/wiki/Battle_of_Coruscant "Battle of Coruscant") in order to lure Skywalker to the dark side. The Jedi calculated a decisive Republic victory through the destruction of General [Grievous](/wiki/Grievous "Grievous"), which was achieved by Obi-Wan Kenobi during the [Battle of Utapau](/wiki/Battle_of_Utapau "Battle of Utapau"). However, Skywalker, whose turmoil clouded his judgment, learned that Palpatine was Sidious. Though he informed Windu of Palpatine's identity, Sidious resisted the Jedi's efforts to arrest him, killing three Jedi Masters—Kit Fisto, [Agen Kolar](/wiki/Agen_Kolar "Agen Kolar"), and [Saesee Tiin](/wiki/Saesee_Tiin "Saesee Tiin")—forcing Windu to [duel](/wiki/Duel_in_Palpatine%27s_office "Duel in Palpatine's office") the Dark Lord alone. Skywalker rushed to [Palpatine's office](/wiki/Palpatine%27s_office "Palpatine's office") as Windu and the chancellor fought, arriving moments after the Jedi champion disarmed the Sith Lord. Before Windu could kill Sidious, Skywalker betrayed him by severing his hand, which led to the Jedi Master's death. Believing Sidious had the power to save his [secret wife](/wiki/Wedding_of_Anakin_Skywalker_and_Padm%C3%A9_Amidala "Wedding of Anakin Skywalker and Padmé Amidala"), Padmé Amidala, Skywalker betrayed the Jedi and became Sidious' apprentice, and was given the name of Darth Vader.[[19]](#cite_note-Episode_III-19)

### The purge[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Order 66](/wiki/Order_66 "Order 66")
:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Great Jedi Purge](/wiki/Great_Jedi_Purge "Great Jedi Purge")

:   "*A young Jedi named Darth Vader, who was a pupil of mine until he turned to evil, helped the Empire hunt down and destroy the Jedi Knights. He betrayed and murdered your father. Now the Jedi are all but extinct.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi, to Luke Skywalker[[44]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-44)

 [![Converted to the dark side, Anakin Skywalker led the Great Jedi Purge as the Sith Lord Darth Vader.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/58/MissionToMustafar-2020DarthVader7.png/revision/latest?cb=20210531064227) [![Converted to the dark side, Anakin Skywalker led the Great Jedi Purge as the Sith Lord Darth Vader.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/58/MissionToMustafar-2020DarthVader7.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20210531064227)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/58/MissionToMustafar-2020DarthVader7.png/revision/latest?cb=20210531064227) 

Converted to the dark side, Anakin Skywalker led the Great Jedi Purge as the Sith Lord Darth Vader.

 

Branding Windu's actions as treason, Palpatine declared the Jedi to be enemies of the Republic and sent Vader to oversee the [siege of the Jedi Temple](/wiki/Operation:_Knightfall "Operation: Knightfall"). As his new apprentice purged the Temple of its inhabitants, including the younglings, Sidious had his Clone Commanders to execute Order 66, thereby activating the biochips that programmed the clones to see the Jedi as traitors to the Republic. As a result, thousands of Jedi throughout the galaxy were betrayed and executed by their clones including Ki-Adi-Mundi on [Mygeeto](/wiki/Mygeeto "Mygeeto"), Aayla Secura on Felucia, [Plo Koon](/wiki/Plo_Koon "Plo Koon") on [Cato Neimoidia](/wiki/Cato_Neimoidia "Cato Neimoidia"), [Stass Allie](/wiki/Stass_Allie "Stass Allie") on [Saleucami](/wiki/Saleucami "Saleucami"),[[19]](#cite_note-Episode_III-19) [Depa Billaba](/wiki/Depa_Billaba "Depa Billaba") on [Kaller](/wiki/Kaller "Kaller"),[[211]](#cite_note-Kanan_2-211) and [Jaro Tapal](/wiki/Jaro_Tapal "Jaro Tapal") above [Bracca](/wiki/Bracca "Bracca").[[212]](#cite_note-Jedi:_Fallen_Order-212)

Out of an estimated number of ten-thousand Jedi,[[71]](#cite_note-PotJ-71)[[70]](#cite_note-Tarkin-70)[[213]](#cite_note-AND-213)[[214]](#cite_note-Siege-214) just a few survived to see the [proclamation of the New Order](/wiki/Proclamation_of_the_New_Order "Proclamation of the New Order"), marking the inception of the Galactic Empire and the rise of Palpatine as its [Emperor](/wiki/Emperor "Emperor").[[19]](#cite_note-Episode_III-19) Survivors included Yoda,[[94]](#cite_note-Episode_V-94) Obi-Wan Kenobi,[[44]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-44) Ahsoka Tano,[[215]](#cite_note-FAtG-215) [Caleb Dume](/wiki/Kanan_Jarrus "Kanan Jarrus"),[[213]](#cite_note-AND-213) [Cal Kestis](/wiki/Cal_Kestis "Cal Kestis"), [Cere Junda](/wiki/Cere_Junda "Cere Junda") and her Padawan [Trilla Suduri](/wiki/Second_Sister "Second Sister"), [Taron Malicos](/wiki/Taron_Malicos "Taron Malicos"),[[212]](#cite_note-Jedi:_Fallen_Order-212) and at least initially, [Uvell](/wiki/Uvell "Uvell"),[[216]](#cite_note-TEoH-216) Luminara Unduli,[[217]](#cite_note-RotOM-217) [Oppo Rancisis](/wiki/Oppo_Rancisis "Oppo Rancisis"), [Eeth Koth](/wiki/Eeth_Koth "Eeth Koth"), [Coleman Kcaj](/wiki/Coleman_Kcaj "Coleman Kcaj"),[[218]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_19-218) [Jocasta Nu](/wiki/Jocasta_Nu "Jocasta Nu"),[[219]](#cite_note-Dying_Light_I-219) [Kirak Infil'a](/wiki/Kirak_Infil%27a "Kirak Infil'a"),[[26]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_2-26) [Selrahc Eluos](/wiki/Selrahc_Eluos "Selrahc Eluos"), [Ka-Moon Kholi](/wiki/Ka-Moon_Kholi "Ka-Moon Kholi"), [Zubain Ankonori](/wiki/Zubain_Ankonori "Zubain Ankonori"), [Khandra](/wiki/Khandra "Khandra"), [Mususiel](/wiki/Mususiel "Mususiel"), [Nuhj](/wiki/Nuhj "Nuhj"), [Ferren Barr](/wiki/Ferren_Barr "Ferren Barr"), and possibly [Quinlan Vos](/wiki/Quinlan_Vos "Quinlan Vos").[[219]](#cite_note-Dying_Light_I-219) During their self-imposed exile, Kenobi and Yoda, along with Senator [Bail Organa](/wiki/Bail_Prestor_Organa "Bail Prestor Organa"), hid Vader's newborn children, the Force-sensitive [twins](/wiki/Twin "Twin") Luke Skywalker and [Leia Organa](/wiki/Leia_Skywalker_Organa_Solo "Leia Skywalker Organa Solo"), from the Sith, hoping that in time they would become the key to the Jedi Order's future to stop the dark side.[[158]](#cite_note-Sacrifice-158)[[19]](#cite_note-Episode_III-19)

 [![The Galactic Empire hunted the few remaining Jedi who survived the initial execution of Order 66.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0c/CalebEscapesClones-Kanan2.png/revision/latest?cb=20210625033918) [![The Galactic Empire hunted the few remaining Jedi who survived the initial execution of Order 66.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0c/CalebEscapesClones-Kanan2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20210625033918)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0c/CalebEscapesClones-Kanan2.png/revision/latest?cb=20210625033918) 

The Galactic Empire hunted the few remaining Jedi who survived the initial execution of Order 66.

 

Word about the supposed Jedi rebellion and the Order's destruction spread throughout the galactic population, and clone troopers were ordered to hunt down any Jedi survivors.[[211]](#cite_note-Kanan_2-211) According to Imperial Admiral [Rae Sloane](/wiki/Rae_Sloane "Rae Sloane"), the Jedi that had survived Order 66 made a [last stand](/wiki/Jedi_survivors%27_last_stand "Jedi survivors' last stand") against a clone trooper charge led personally by the future war veteran and [Shadow Council](/wiki/Shadow_Council "Shadow Council") member [Hodnar Borrum](/wiki/Hodnar_Borrum "Hodnar Borrum"), who was known to hold disdain for the Force, on a [mountain](/wiki/Mountain "Mountain") fortress on either [Madar](/wiki/Madar "Madar") or [Morad](/wiki/Morad "Morad").[[220]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-220) Palpatine squarely blamed the Jedi for the galaxy's recent crises[[134]](#cite_note-Launchpad229-134) and painted them as warmongers whose planned coup[[124]](#cite_note-Crimson_Reign_3-124) involved creating the Separatist Alliance[[135]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_1-135) and Clone Wars in the first place.[[124]](#cite_note-Crimson_Reign_3-124) Relieved to see the bloody war over at last and eager for any sense of normalcy to resume, the populous embraced Palpatine's empire, with most of the galaxy blasting the Jedi for their alleged betrayal or even simply because they had failed to prevent, or effectively win, the war.[[196]](#cite_note-MoF-196)

In addition to the Empire's suppression of all information relating to the Jedi, it was considered treasonous to be a Jedi or render assistance to a Jedi. Imperial laws also prohibited the use or study of the Force, resulting in the banning of educational studies concerning the Jedi. As a consequence, instructors who specialized in Jedi history lost their positions,[[124]](#cite_note-Crimson_Reign_3-124) including [Sava](/wiki/Sava "Sava") [Korin Pers](/wiki/Korin_Pers "Korin Pers")[[221]](#cite_note-Lando_3-221) and Sava Madelin Sun from the [University of Bar'leth](/wiki/University_of_Bar%27leth "University of Bar'leth").[[124]](#cite_note-Crimson_Reign_3-124) Within five years of the Order's destruction,[[70]](#cite_note-Tarkin-70) the Jedi were effectively erased from the collective consciousness in the galaxy due to the [Great Jedi Purge](/wiki/Great_Jedi_Purge "Great Jedi Purge"),[[124]](#cite_note-Crimson_Reign_3-124) which also involved the systematic destruction of their temples[[71]](#cite_note-PotJ-71) and the unceasing, extensive hunts carried out by the [Inquisitorius](/wiki/Inquisitorius "Inquisitorius").[[222]](#cite_note-AEYNTK-222)

Jedi survivors that were captured were taken to [Mustafar](/wiki/Mustafar "Mustafar") for interrogation and execution,[[223]](#cite_note-DB-mustafar-223)[[215]](#cite_note-FAtG-215) as well as the [Spire](/wiki/Spire_(Stygeon_Prime) "Spire (Stygeon Prime)") on [Stygeon Prime](/wiki/Stygeon_Prime "Stygeon Prime"), wherein the body of Luminara Unduli was preserved to lure out any surviving Jedi.[[217]](#cite_note-RotOM-217) Among the last reservoirs of knowledge of the Order were [Antron Bach](/wiki/Antron_Bach "Antron Bach")'s vault in an abandoned [colony](/wiki/Unidentified_Geonosian_colony "Unidentified Geonosian colony"), created at Uvell's behest,[[216]](#cite_note-TEoH-216) and [Grakkus](/wiki/Grakkus_Jahibakti_Tingi "Grakkus Jahibakti Tingi") the [Hutt](/wiki/Hutt "Hutt")'s private collection on [Nar Shaddaa](/wiki/Nar_Shaddaa "Nar Shaddaa").[[74]](#cite_note-SW9-74)[[224]](#cite_note-SW10-224) Safeguarding holocrons, lightsabers, journals, archives, and other artifacts, they partially preserved the teachings of the fallen Order.[[216]](#cite_note-TEoH-216)[[74]](#cite_note-SW9-74) The surviving Jedi [Nedriss Narr](/wiki/Nedriss_Narr "Nedriss Narr") and [Vanzell Mar-Klar](/wiki/Vanzell_Mar-Klar "Vanzell Mar-Klar") attempted to train new younglings in a secret temple.[[225]](#cite_note-Trials-225)

### Dark times[]

#### Fallen order[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main articles: [Investigation into the framing of the Jedi](/wiki/Investigation_into_the_framing_of_the_Jedi "Investigation into the framing of the Jedi"), [Secret mission to rebuild the Jedi Order](/wiki/Secret_mission_to_rebuild_the_Jedi_Order "Secret mission to rebuild the Jedi Order") and [Hunt for Tensu Run](/wiki/Hunt_for_Tensu_Run "Hunt for Tensu Run")

:   "*The Jedi were* good*. Like all of us, they failed to secure the peace. They were drawn into the war like everyone else, and their hands were* not *clean. If I can accept the blame for my part, they certainly earned their share, too.* But *for thousands of years they could have ruled the galaxy, and instead they chose to serve. They had their own vested interests, their own ways of politicking. But they believed their power came with an obligation to live humbly, to do good without asserting authority. Maybe they failed to live up to those ideals in the end. I haven't seen your evidence. What do* I *know about the extent of their betrayals? But they were good and they were ordinary and they were fallible, and even the most smug and arrogant were trying to hew to a tradition older than the Republic. They deserved better than to die at the hands of power-hungry old men who saw them as a threat.* We *deserved better than to lose another people, another religion, from the universe. All of us are poorer for their loss.* […] *The Jedi deserve justice… or at least a decent funeral.*"
:   ―Mon Mothma, to [Soujen Vak-Nhalis](/wiki/Soujen_Vak-Nhalis "Soujen Vak-Nhalis")[[196]](#cite_note-MoF-196)

For nearly twenty years, the Empire was able to expand without opposition of a disbanded Jedi Order. A few of its former members, however survived and stayed true to their code of honor and continued to fight the Empire's injustice, albeit in different ways. Though former Padawan Ahsoka Tano had become disillusioned by the Council's actions and no longer identified as a Jedi, she came into contact with Bail Organa from [Alderaan](/wiki/Alderaan "Alderaan"), with whom she worked to coordinate the efforts of a rebellion under the codename "Fulcrum," fifteen years after the fall of the Republic.[[215]](#cite_note-FAtG-215)

 [![Having survived the execution of Order 66, Padawan Cal Kestis endeavored to resurrect the fallen Jedi Order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/50/CalHolocronList.png/revision/latest?cb=20200513152033) [![Having survived the execution of Order 66, Padawan Cal Kestis endeavored to resurrect the fallen Jedi Order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/50/CalHolocronList.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200513152033)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/50/CalHolocronList.png/revision/latest?cb=20200513152033) 

Having survived the execution of Order 66, Padawan Cal Kestis endeavored to resurrect the fallen Jedi Order.

 

Five years after the rise of the Empire and the destruction of the Jedi Order, there was an attempt to bring the Order back. Padawan Cal Kestis, who had been hiding on Bracca since Order 66, was recruited by the former Jedi Knight Cere Junda, who believed that the return of the Jedi Order was the best option to defeat the Empire. Having spent so long in hiding due to the persecution of the Jedi, Kestis did not trust Junda at first, suspecting that she might have come to him out of interest in the rewards offered by the Empire. Despite this, he joined her in her [mission to rebuild the Order](/wiki/Secret_mission_to_rebuild_the_Jedi_Order "Secret mission to rebuild the Jedi Order"). To accomplish this, they sought to recover a [holocron](/wiki/Eno_Cordova%27s_holocron "Eno Cordova's holocron") that had been hidden on the planet [Bogano](/wiki/Bogano "Bogano") by Jedi Master [Eno Cordova](/wiki/Eno_Cordova "Eno Cordova"). This holocron contained a list of the locations of Force-sensitive children across the galaxy.[[212]](#cite_note-Jedi:_Fallen_Order-212)

After scouring ancient ruins for clues left behind by the extinct [Zeffo civilization](/wiki/Zeffonian "Zeffonian"), Kestis succeeded in unlocking the [Vault](/wiki/Bogano_Vault "Bogano Vault") that contained the holocron, but the artifact was taken by the [Second Sister](/wiki/Second_Sister "Second Sister"), an Inquisitor who had been Junda's Padawan before the Purge. Junda proclaimed Kestis a Jedi Knight, and together they [pursued](/wiki/Mission_to_Nur "Mission to Nur") the Second Sister to the [Fortress Inquisitorius](/wiki/Fortress_Inquisitorius "Fortress Inquisitorius") on the [ocean](/wiki/Ocean "Ocean") moon [Nur](/wiki/Nur "Nur"). They succeeded in retrieving the holocron from the Second Sister, who was executed by Darth Vader. The Dark Lord overpowered both Jedi, wounded Kestis for refusing to surrender the holocron, and goaded Junda to embrace the dark side. Ultimately, though, Kestis and Junda managed to escape from Vader with their [allies'](/wiki/Stinger_Mantis_crew "Stinger Mantis crew") help. Despite Kestis' commitment to the restoration of the Jedi Order, the young Jedi Knight destroyed the holocron to protect the Force-sensitive younglings, entrusting their fate to the will of the Force.[[212]](#cite_note-Jedi:_Fallen_Order-212)

 [![Along with other survivors, Jedi Knight Tensu Run aimed to restore the Jedi Order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4b/TensuJedPanZayron-Inquisitors1.png/revision/latest?cb=20241217002812) [![Along with other survivors, Jedi Knight Tensu Run aimed to restore the Jedi Order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4b/TensuJedPanZayron-Inquisitors1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20241217002812)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4b/TensuJedPanZayron-Inquisitors1.png/revision/latest?cb=20241217002812) 

Along with other survivors, Jedi Knight Tensu Run aimed to restore the Jedi Order.

 

Jedi Knight [Tensu Run](/wiki/Tensu_Run "Tensu Run") became a threat to the Empire, as after freeing prisoners from an [Imperial outpost](/wiki/Imperial_outpost_(Regis_Kor) "Imperial outpost (Regis Kor)") during the [Conquest of Regis Kor](/wiki/Conquest_of_Regis_Kor "Conquest of Regis Kor"), he became a symbol of hope. Tensu Run's [death](/wiki/Death "Death") became one of the Inquisitorius' highest priorities, with [the Grand Inquisitor](/wiki/The_Grand_Inquisitor "The Grand Inquisitor"),[[226]](#cite_note-Inquisitors_1-226) the [Fifth Brother](/wiki/Fifth_Brother "Fifth Brother"),[[227]](#cite_note-Inquisitors_2-227) the [Seventh Sister](/wiki/Seventh_Sister "Seventh Sister") and the [Ninth Sister](/wiki/Ninth_Sister "Ninth Sister"),[[228]](#cite_note-Inquisitors_3-228) all participating in the [hunt](/wiki/Hunt_for_Tensu_Run "Hunt for Tensu Run"). The Inquisitors were defeated more than once by the Jedi Knight, who, along with other survivors of Order 66, sought to restore the Jedi Order. Due to the Inquisitors' failures, Darth Vader led the four Inquisitors in a final confrontation with the Jedi, which resulted in Run's death by the hands of the Sith Lord, as well as the other Jedi, who were killed by the Inquisitors.[[229]](#cite_note-Inquisitors_4-229)

#### Rediscovery of an abandoned world[]

:   "*Tanalorr's a fortress. We should use it for the Hidden Path. Gather allies. Train. They'd never see us coming.*"
:   ―Cal Kestis[[230]](#cite_note-Jedi:_Survivor-230)

 [![Hidden in the deadly Koboh Abyss nebula, Tanalorr was a world that was abandoned by the Jedi Order and could have proven to be its future.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/36/Tanalorr_SWJediSurvivor.png/revision/latest?cb=20230429060921) [![Hidden in the deadly Koboh Abyss nebula, Tanalorr was a world that was abandoned by the Jedi Order and could have proven to be its future.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/36/Tanalorr_SWJediSurvivor.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/184?cb=20230429060921)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/36/Tanalorr_SWJediSurvivor.png/revision/latest?cb=20230429060921) 

Hidden in the deadly Koboh Abyss nebula, Tanalorr was a world that was abandoned by the Jedi Order and could have proven to be its future.

 

Over the five years following the holocron's destruction, Kestis had become an extremely important target for the Empire, having attracted the attention of not only the Inquisitorius but also the [Imperial Security Bureau](/wiki/Imperial_Security_Bureau "Imperial Security Bureau") through his [crusade against the Empire](/wiki/Stinger_Mantis_crew%27s_crusade_against_the_Empire "Stinger Mantis crew's crusade against the Empire"). In [9 BBY](/wiki/9_BBY "9 BBY"), on the planet [Koboh](/wiki/Koboh "Koboh"), Kestis encountered something from the Jedi's golden ag;. Kestis encountered the Jedi [Dagan Gera](/wiki/Dagan_Gera "Dagan Gera"), who had been preserved in bacta since the days of the High Republic. Kestis freed the old Jedi and asked for his help in his fight against the Empire. However, Gera had fallen out with the Jedi Order, which he believed had betrayed him because the Jedi had given up on [Tanalorr](/wiki/Tanalorr "Tanalorr"), a hard-to-reach world Dagan had become obsessed with, after an [attack](/wiki/Attack_on_Tanalorr "Attack on Tanalorr") by the [Nihil](/wiki/Nihil "Nihil"). Gera, who had fallen to the dark side, bled the kyber crystal from his lightsaber and began a duel with Kestis.[[230]](#cite_note-Jedi:_Survivor-230)

Dagan escaped with the help of his old ally, the [Gen'Dai](/wiki/Gen%27Dai "Gen'Dai") [Rayvis](/wiki/Rayvis "Rayvis"), and intended to return to Tanalorr and create an army led by Force users trained by himself to fight the Empire. However, due to the clouded view of Gera by the dark side, Kestis opposed his plan. Along with [Bode Akuna](/wiki/Bode_Akuna "Bode Akuna"), Kestis killed Dagan and obtained the compass that would guide them to Tanalorr, a place that Kestis intended to transform into a refuge for those persecuted by the Empire.[[230]](#cite_note-Jedi:_Survivor-230)

 [![Cere Junda's death left Jedi Cal Kestis determined to build something that would outlast the Empire.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/09/Cere_Junda_lightsaber_hilt.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20231029010815) [![Cere Junda's death left Jedi Cal Kestis determined to build something that would outlast the Empire.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/09/Cere_Junda_lightsaber_hilt.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/221?cb=20231029010815)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/09/Cere_Junda_lightsaber_hilt.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20231029010815) 

Cere Junda's death left Jedi Cal Kestis determined to build something that would outlast the Empire.

 

However, the compass was stolen by Akuna, who was another survivor of the Jedi Purge and had begun working with the ISB as a spy to survive. Akuna intended to flee to Tanalorr with he daughter so that they could live free from the Empire forever, which, in he opinion, Kestis' intentions for Tanalorr jeopardized. Kestis followed Akuna to Tanalorr, and along with his ally, the [Nightsister](/wiki/Nightsisters "Nightsisters") [Merrin](/wiki/Merrin "Merrin"), slew him. Kestis and his friends took in Bode's daughter and held a Jedi funeral for Akuna, Cere Junda, and Eno Cordova, who were trying to restore knowledge from the Jedi archives and were killed due to Akuna stealing the compass. With the compass in their possession, Kestis and his allies began to prepare Tanalorr for use in the [Hidden Path](/wiki/Hidden_Path "Hidden Path")'s operations.[[230]](#cite_note-Jedi:_Survivor-230)

#### Rebellion and war[]

:   "*Things are getting worse, just as they did when I was your age. But back then, there were ten thousand Jedi protecting the galaxy. Now…*"  
    "*There's just you and me.*"
:   ―Kanan Jarrus and Ezra Bridger[[214]](#cite_note-Siege-214)

 [![The Jedi Kanan Jarrus and Ezra Bridger supported the early Rebellion against the Empire.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4e/Rebels_protect_Trayvis.png/revision/latest?cb=20150127160710) [![The Jedi Kanan Jarrus and Ezra Bridger supported the early Rebellion against the Empire.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4e/Rebels_protect_Trayvis.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150127160710)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4e/Rebels_protect_Trayvis.png/revision/latest?cb=20150127160710) 

The Jedi Kanan Jarrus and Ezra Bridger supported the early Rebellion against the Empire.

 

Eight years after the end of the Clone Wars, Caleb Dume, who had assumed the identity of Kanan Jarrus, joined forces with the Twi'lek rebel fighter [Hera Syndulla](/wiki/Hera_Syndulla "Hera Syndulla").[[213]](#cite_note-AND-213) Together, the two established a [small rebel cell](/wiki/Spectres "Spectres") based on the starship *[Ghost](/wiki/Ghost "Ghost")*.[[231]](#cite_note-Spark-231) Fifteen years into the [Imperial Era](/wiki/Imperial_Era "Imperial Era"), a number of inaccurate tales about the Jedi started to appear. For example, the bounty hunter duo [Gowski](/wiki/Gowski "Gowski") and Fiscal were under the impression that Jedi aged backward, were able to fly, and had unusually dense [bones](/wiki/Bone "Bone").[[232]](#cite_note-EotP-232) About five years before the Battle of Yavin, Jarrus took on a Force-sensitive teenager named [Ezra Bridger](/wiki/Ezra_Bridger "Ezra Bridger") as his apprentice.[[231]](#cite_note-Spark-231)

Jarrus' [decision to ignite](/wiki/Mission_to_free_Wookiee_prisoners "Mission to free Wookiee prisoners") [his lightsaber](/wiki/Kanan_Jarrus%27_lightsaber "Kanan Jarrus' lightsaber") on [Kessel](/wiki/Kessel "Kessel") drew the attention of [the Grand Inquisitor](/wiki/The_Grand_Inquisitor "The Grand Inquisitor"), whom Vader had tasked with hunting down Jedi and recruiting the "children of the Force."[[231]](#cite_note-Spark-231) Under Jarrus' tutelage, Bridger trained as a Jedi while evading the Grand Inquisitor and other Imperial agents.[[233]](#cite_note-Gathering_Forces-233) Bridger completed his Jedi Trials at the Lothal Jedi Temple under the guidance of Master Yoda, who also counseled Jarrus to continue training Bridger.[[71]](#cite_note-PotJ-71) At the instigation of [Grand Moff](/wiki/Grand_Moff "Grand Moff") [Wilhuff Tarkin](/wiki/Wilhuff_Tarkin "Wilhuff Tarkin"), the Grand Inquisitor and [Agent](/wiki/Agent "Agent") [Alexsandr Kallus](/wiki/Alexsandr_Kallus "Alexsandr Kallus") concocted a [trap](/wiki/Raid_on_the_communications_tower "Raid on the communications tower") that captured Jarrus. However, Bridger and the other rebels mounted a [mission](/wiki/Action_at_Mustafar "Action at Mustafar") to rescue Jarrus and killed the Grand Inquisitor. In the process, they encountered other members of the rebellion including the former Padawan Ahsoka Tano, who had become a key rebel leader.[[215]](#cite_note-FAtG-215)

### Return of the Jedi[]

:   "*You failed, your Highness. I am a Jedi, like my father before me.*"
:   ―Luke Skywalker, to Darth Sidious[[35]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-35)

During a mission, they inspired not only the people of Lothal to fight the Empire, but also the early "Alliance" to finally organize and to bring several Rebel cells together, paving the way for the Alliance to Restore the Republic.[[215]](#cite_note-FAtG-215) An underground faith known as the [Church of the Force](/wiki/Church_of_the_Force "Church of the Force") emerged in support of the Jedi and their ideals, believing that only their return could restore balance to the Force.[[159]](#cite_note-tfa-TVD-159)

 [![The galaxy found a new hope in Anakin Skywalker's son, Luke Skywalker, who became a Jedi like his father before him.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/22/Thoseabouttojediwesaluteyou.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120111033259) [![The galaxy found a new hope in Anakin Skywalker's son, Luke Skywalker, who became a Jedi like his father before him.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/22/Thoseabouttojediwesaluteyou.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20120111033259)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/22/Thoseabouttojediwesaluteyou.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120111033259) 

The galaxy found a new hope in Anakin Skywalker's son, Luke Skywalker, who became a Jedi like his father before him.

 

In [1 BBY](/wiki/1_BBY "1 BBY"),[[234]](#cite_note-Galactic_Atlas_Updated-234) Obi-Wan Kenobi emerged from his exile on Tatooine, not only to help [deliver](/wiki/Secret_mission_to_Tatooine "Secret mission to Tatooine") the [plans](/wiki/Death_Star_plans "Death Star plans") of the [Death Star](/wiki/DS-1_Orbital_Battle_Station "DS-1 Orbital Battle Station") to the Rebel Alliance as requested by Rebel leader Princess Leia Organa but to begin training Luke Skywalker to become a Jedi Knight,[[44]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-44) in the hopes that Skywalker would be able to defeat both Vader and the Emperor.[[35]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-35) Through Skywalker, with Kenobi's [guidance](/wiki/Force_spirit "Force spirit"), the Rebel Alliance achieved a significant victory in the Battle of Yavin, which meant a turning point for the Alliance in the [Galactic Civil War](/wiki/Galactic_Civil_War "Galactic Civil War"), though at the cost of Kenobi who sacrificed himself to save Skywalker.[[44]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-44) In [3 ABY](/wiki/3_ABY "3 ABY"),[[40]](#cite_note-Galactic_Atlas-40) Skywalker received training from Yoda on [Dagobah](/wiki/Dagobah "Dagobah").[[94]](#cite_note-Episode_V-94) Hailed as "the last of the Jedi," Skywalker was told by Yoda to pass on what he had learned so that the legacy of the Jedi Order could go on, before passing.[[35]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-35)

Forced to duel Vader while Sidious watched during the [Battle of Endor](/wiki/Battle_of_Endor "Battle of Endor"), Skywalker briefly gave into anger and fear and cut off his father's hand. Satisfied, Sidious betrayed Vader by ordering Luke to take his place on Sidious' side, but Skywalker rejected his anger and proclaimed he would always remain a Jedi, which led to him being [tortured](/wiki/Force_lightning "Force lightning") by the furious Emperor. In agony, he begged his father to save him, convincing the former Anakin Skywalker to save his son, leading to the redeemed Jedi Knight to destroy his master. By destroying his master and the Sith,[[35]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-35) Anakin brought balance to the Force for the time being,[[235]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-235) ultimately fulfilling his role as the Chosen One. While the injuries he sustained in the process of destroying Sidious, led to his death shortly after, Anakin made peace with Luke before passing and becoming a [Force ghost](/wiki/Force_spirit "Force spirit") alongside Yoda and Obi-Wan,[[35]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-35) who assured him that his son likely had a bright future ahead.[[236]](#cite_note-Line_Webtoon-236)

After the [Battle of Jakku](/wiki/Battle_of_Jakku "Battle of Jakku"), the Empire officially [surrendered](/wiki/Imperial_Instruments_of_Surrender "Imperial Instruments of Surrender") to the [New Republic](/wiki/New_Republic "New Republic") by way of the [Galactic Concordance](/wiki/Galactic_Concordance "Galactic Concordance"), which put strict provisions on the rump state.[[159]](#cite_note-tfa-TVD-159) In the [Unknown Regions](/wiki/Unknown_Regions "Unknown Regions"), however, fleeing [Imperial officers](/wiki/Imperial_officer "Imperial officer") and [nobles](/wiki/Noble "Noble") conspired to rebuild their armies and [fleets](/wiki/Fleet "Fleet"), culminating in the rise of the hermetic [First Order](/wiki/First_Order "First Order").[[38]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-38) In the meantime, Skywalker gained a new ally in an individual named [Lor San Tekka](/wiki/Lor_San_Tekka "Lor San Tekka"), a member of the Church of the Force during the dark times,[[159]](#cite_note-tfa-TVD-159) who believed the return of the Jedi was necessary to have balance in the Force[[38]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-38) and aided Skywalker in retrieving lost Jedi lore.[[237]](#cite_note-DB_San_Tekka-237)

### An order reborn[]

#### Stumbled Beginnings[]

:   "*After the Empire fell and the Sith Lords were vanquished, I had great hope for the future of the Jedi. I came to believe that if a single Jedi could help bring balance back to the Force, then perhaps a restored Jedi Order could maintain that peace and prevent the dark side from ever regaining its hold on the galaxy.*"
:   ―Luke Skywalker[[62]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Jedi-62)

 [![As the last Jedi, Skywalker carried the mandate of restoring the Jedi Order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/06/Luke-Leia-training.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200613205339) [![As the last Jedi, Skywalker carried the mandate of restoring the Jedi Order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/06/Luke-Leia-training.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200613205339)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/06/Luke-Leia-training.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200613205339) 

As the last Jedi, Skywalker carried the mandate of restoring the Jedi Order.

 

Following the Battle of Endor, the Alliance General Han Solo and the former [Princess](/wiki/Princess "Princess") of Alderaan, Leia Organa, were [married](/wiki/Wedding_of_Han_Solo_and_Leia_Organa "Wedding of Han Solo and Leia Organa")[[220]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-220) and after the final defeat of the Empire at [Jakku](/wiki/Jakku "Jakku"), they had a son named [Ben Solo](/wiki/Ben_Solo "Ben Solo").[[7]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-7) Ben was Luke Skywalker's nephew,[[38]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-38) as Organa was his twin sister, a fact Skywalker only learned from the Force spirit of Obi-Wan Kenobi following Yoda's death.[[35]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-35) Before her wedding, Skywalker had spoken to Organa about training her and affirmed that she did not need to give up her marriage to Solo if she went down the Jedi path. While at first she still feared she would nevertheless have to choose between her marriage or that path,[[108]](#cite_note-The_Princess_and_the_Scoundrel-108) she would agree to become her brother's pupil. On [Ajan Kloss](/wiki/Ajan_Kloss "Ajan Kloss"), Skywalker trained Organa in the ways of the Jedi as his first student.[[65]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-65) She even constructed [her own lightsaber](/wiki/Leia%27s_lightsaber "Leia's lightsaber"), but after seeing a vision of her son's death as the culmination of her Jedi training, Organa declined to progress further. She then directed her focus to the future of the New Republic.[[235]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-235)

Around [five years](/wiki/9_ABY "9 ABY") after the Battle of Endor, Skywalker helped rescue Grogu, a mysterious child of the same species as Yoda, survivor of the siege of the Jedi Temple and who had performed great feats in the Force. Skywalker expressed his desire to train the child in the ways of the Force and took Grogu in with the approval of the child's protector, the Mandalorian [Din Djarin](/wiki/Din_Djarin "Din Djarin").[[238]](#cite_note-Chapter_16-238) With Ahsoka Tano helping to oversee the effort,[[80]](#cite_note-From_the_Desert_Comes_a_Stranger-80) the Jedi Temple of Luke Skywalker was founded as a training center when Skywalker attempted to restore the Jedi Order,[[18]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-18) with Grogu becoming Skywalker's first student. After Tano parted ways with them for the time being, Skywalker gave Grogu a choice; he could remain with his new Jedi Order or return to Din Djarin.[[80]](#cite_note-From_the_Desert_Comes_a_Stranger-80) Grogu chose to return to Djarin, ending his Jedi training and having Skywalker send R2-D2 to pilot Grogu to Tatooine to reunite him with Djarin.[[239]](#cite_note-In_the_Name_of_Honor-239)

#### A new generation[]

:   "*For many years, there was balance and then I saw Ben. My nephew with that mighty Skywalker blood. In my hubris, I thought I could train him; I could pass on my strengths. Han was* Han *about it, but… Leia trusted me with her son. I took him and a dozen students, and began a training temple.*"
:   ―Luke Skywalker, to Rey[[18]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-18)

Although Skywalker regarded Kenobi and Yoda as the greatest masters in Jedi history, he knew that his training was unorthodox. As a Jedi Master, Skywalker aimed to provide his apprentices with a more traditional approach to the Jedi arts, and as such, his Padawans followed a training regime similar to the one that existed during the Republic Era.[[62]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Jedi-62) The New Jedi Order began as a class of Force-sensitive younglings, beginning with Skywalker's nephew, Ben Solo,[[240]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_3-240) whom he agreed to train in the ways of the Force at his sister's behest. In many ways, Solo reminded his parents of his grandfather, Darth Vader, therefore Organa wanted him to train with his uncle in the hope that he would not turn to the dark side as well.[[38]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-38)

 [![Skywalker founded a temple where he could train a new generation of Jedi apprentices, including his nephew Ben Solo.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/LukeTeachingJedi-TheRiseOfKyloRen3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20250306232725) [![Skywalker founded a temple where he could train a new generation of Jedi apprentices, including his nephew Ben Solo.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/LukeTeachingJedi-TheRiseOfKyloRen3.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250306232725)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/LukeTeachingJedi-TheRiseOfKyloRen3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20250306232725) 

Skywalker founded a temple where he could train a new generation of Jedi apprentices, including his nephew Ben Solo.

 

In addition to Solo, Skywalker recruited several other students including [Hennix](/wiki/Hennix "Hennix"), [Tai](/wiki/Tai "Tai"), and [Voe](/wiki/Voe "Voe")[[241]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_1-241) during his visits to many worlds over two [decades](/wiki/Standard_decade "Standard decade").[[14]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-14) During this time, Solo was trained in lightsaber combat and became skilled with the Jedi weapon.[[159]](#cite_note-tfa-TVD-159) In [19 ABY,](/wiki/19_ABY "19 ABY") Skywalker traveled with his nephew and Lor San Tekka to the Jedi outpost on Elphrona seeking Jedi artifacts. The trio were accosted by a dark side sect known as the [Knights of Ren](/wiki/Knights_of_Ren "Knights of Ren"). Master Skywalker used his Force powers to defeat the Knights. Before leaving, the Knights' leader [Ren](/wiki/Ren_(human) "Ren (human)") told Solo to contact the Knights should he ever consider exploring the dark side further.[[75]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_2-75)

By [21 ABY](/wiki/21_ABY "21 ABY"),[[242]](#cite_note-21_ABY_Note-242) the new Jedi Order had grown to the point where it already had senior pupils on top of a new class of younglings in training. Around this time, Luke Skywalker experienced visions that distracted him from some of his basic duties at the academy, leaving some of his senior students to take over for him on this duties. A Twi'lek woman named [Enyo](/wiki/Enyo "Enyo") served as an instructor on lightsaber combat, running a class of younglings through a series of exercises with [training blades](/wiki/Training_lightsaber "Training lightsaber"). When Skywalker went on a mission with Lor San Tekka that distanced him from his temple, Ben Solo, who had also taken the duties of running training exercises on the younger students, stayed to oversee the academy.[[81]](#cite_note-Shadow_of_the_Sith-81)

#### The temple's destruction[]

:   "*I never… I didn't want this.*"  
    "*And you did not choose it, Ben. The* Jedi *did. Skywalker.*"
:   ―Ben Solo and Snoke[[241]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_1-241)

 [![The confrontation between Skywalker and his nephew had fateful consequences for the New Jedi Order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1e/Wakey_wakey_Ben.png/revision/latest?cb=20180510222951) [![The confrontation between Skywalker and his nephew had fateful consequences for the New Jedi Order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1e/Wakey_wakey_Ben.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180510222951)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1e/Wakey_wakey_Ben.png/revision/latest?cb=20180510222951) 

The confrontation between Skywalker and his nephew had fateful consequences for the New Jedi Order.

 

Solo's family would ultimately learn that he was gradually seduced to the ways of the dark side through the machinations of the First Order's ruler, [Supreme Leader](/wiki/Supreme_Leader "Supreme Leader") [Snoke](/wiki/Snoke "Snoke").[[243]](#cite_note-TFA_novel-243) Organa blamed Snoke as the sole cause of her son's descent into darkness, culminating in the [destruction of the Jedi Temple](/wiki/Destruction_of_the_Jedi_Temple "Destruction of the Jedi Temple"), but Skywalker felt responsible for his nephew's fate. Sensing the dark side's influence within Solo, Skywalker probed his nephew's mind and beheld visions of the dark warrior that he was becoming. Skywalker instinctively raised [his lightsaber](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker%27s_green_lightsaber "Luke Skywalker's green lightsaber") to kill his nephew while he slept, believing Solo would destroy all that he loved; however, he stopped himself from killing his sister's son, and was overcome by shame. He then saw that Solo had awoken. He saw fear in the eyes of his young nephew, and in that moment Skywalker felt he had failed as a Jedi Master.[[18]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-18)

Solo reached for his blade and razed the hut using the Force, collapsing it in on his uncle.[[18]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-18) As Solo struggled to comprehend the situation and lost control of his emotions, the Jedi Temple was destroyed by a powerful lightning storm, killing most of Skywalker's other students. Shortly later, Hennix, Tai, and Voe returned from an offworld trip. They confronted Ben Solo, who told them that Skywalker had tried to murder him. Skeptical, they tried to detain him but Solo fled following a brief skirmish and sought Snoke. Hennix, Tai, and Voe resolved to find Solo and investigate what had happened. Meanwhile, Solo sought out Snoke and the two decided to seek out the Knights of Ren.[[241]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_1-241)

 [![With his temple destroyed, Skywalker exiled himself to Ahch-To, vowing to never train another student.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5e/Jedi_massacre_TLJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20180806000935) [![With his temple destroyed, Skywalker exiled himself to Ahch-To, vowing to never train another student.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5e/Jedi_massacre_TLJ.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180806000935)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5e/Jedi_massacre_TLJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20180806000935) 

With his temple destroyed, Skywalker exiled himself to Ahch-To, vowing to never train another student.

 

Skywalker regained consciousness in the rubble of his nephew's hut too late to prevent Solo's destruction of the Jedi temple and the deaths of the students inside. Solo had already fled, and Skywalker could only witness his temple still burning alongside his [astromech droid](/wiki/Astromech_droid "Astromech droid"), [R2-D2](/wiki/R2-D2 "R2-D2").[[18]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-18) Skywalker felt responsible for the ordeal and decided to exile himself, although those closest to him learned that he was also searching for the first Jedi Temple. Skywalker only left traces of his location in a single star [map](/wiki/Map_to_Skywalker "Map to Skywalker"), with the remaining data being present in old Imperial records. Skywalker eventually found the first Jedi temple on the aquatic world of Ahch-To, where he took up refuge and lived in exile as a [hermit](/wiki/Hermit "Hermit").[[38]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-38) Skywalker vowed to never attempt another rebirth of the Jedi Order, and therefore resolved to die as the last Jedi.[[18]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-18)

#### The Jedi Killer[]

:   "*Now you will be who you are. Who you were always meant to be.*"
:   ―Darth Sidious, to Ben Solo[[244]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_4-244)

 [![Rejecting the Jedi and his family, Ben Solo adopted the identity of Kylo Ren.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2c/TheRiseOfKyloRen2_MuirVariantArt.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200101011113) [![Rejecting the Jedi and his family, Ben Solo adopted the identity of Kylo Ren.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2c/TheRiseOfKyloRen2_MuirVariantArt.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20200101011113)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2c/TheRiseOfKyloRen2_MuirVariantArt.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200101011113) 

Rejecting the Jedi and his family, Ben Solo adopted the identity of Kylo Ren.

 

Traveling to the Jedi outpost on Elphrona, Solo contacted Ren, who told him to find the Knights of Ren on Varnak. However, Hennix, Tai and Voe caught up with the fugitive Solo.[[75]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_2-75) Though Tai preferred to reason with Solo, Voe and Hennix [fought](/wiki/Battle_of_Elphrona "Battle of Elphrona") him, believing that he had a role in destroying the Jedi Temple and killing their brethren. Solo killed Hennix in self-defense before fleeing to Varnak. However, Ren was still unsatisfied that Solo was worthy to become a Knight of Ren but took him on a trial run.[[240]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_3-240)

To test Solo's worthiness for the dark side, the Knights of Ren enlisted his services in obtaining a Force relic called the [Mindsplinter](/wiki/Mindsplinter "Mindsplinter") from a group of [Mimbanese](/wiki/Mimbanese "Mimbanese") on the [Minemoon](/wiki/Minemoon "Minemoon"). Using Tai's connection to Solo, Tai and Voe tracked him down there. During the [ensuing skirmish](/wiki/Skirmish_on_the_Minemoon "Skirmish on the Minemoon"), Tai tried to reason with Solo but was murdered by Ren, who deemed him unworthy. Consumed by rage and grief, Solo killed Ren and Voe, embracing the dark side. Taking the path of darkness, Solo became the [master of the Knights of Ren](/wiki/Ren "Ren"), adopting the name "Kylo Ren" and [bleeding](/wiki/Bleeding "Bleeding") his kyber crystal.[[244]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_4-244)

Solo turned to the dark side of the Force and became an apprentice of [Snoke](/wiki/Snoke "Snoke"), joining the First Order and the Knights of Ren in the process and taking on the new identity of Kylo Ren.[[38]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-38) By the time of the outbreak of the First Order/Resistance War, Ren had gained a reputation of a "Jedi killer" due to Ren's skills with [his lightsaber](/wiki/Kylo_Ren%27s_lightsaber "Kylo Ren's lightsaber") and his role in destroying Skywalker's new Jedi and his hopes of fully restoring the Jedi Order.[[159]](#cite_note-tfa-TVD-159) Ren was determined to live up to the legacy of his grandfather,[[38]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-38) whom he considered to be Darth Vader[[245]](#cite_note-DB_Kylo_Ren-245) instead of Anakin Skywalker.[[243]](#cite_note-TFA_novel-243)

### An awakening[]

:   "*If Skywalker returns, the new Jedi will* rise*.*"
:   ―Snoke[[38]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-38)

As Luke Skywalker's efforts to rebuild the Jedi Order had seemingly failed,[[159]](#cite_note-tfa-TVD-159) the Jedi Master's fabled return became a symbol of hope for those who believed in him and the Jedi. For others, he remained a myth, but he also posed a threat for those who feared his reappearance, such as Supreme Leader Snoke and the First Order, who believed Skywalker's return would also mean the rise of the new Jedi. It was by this time that an awakening occurred within the Force. Snoke and Ren both sensed it;[[38]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-38) Snoke was certain that as his apprentice grew stronger with the dark side, his counterpart in the light would rise as well. Convinced that it was Skywalker,[[18]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-18) Snoke directed Ren to seek out and destroy his former master.[[38]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-38)

 [![Ren hunted Skywalker across the galaxy, searching for clues to the whereabouts of his old master.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e3/Lor_San_Tekka_brought_before_Kylo_Ren.png/revision/latest?cb=20190604061240) [![Ren hunted Skywalker across the galaxy, searching for clues to the whereabouts of his old master.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e3/Lor_San_Tekka_brought_before_Kylo_Ren.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190604061240)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e3/Lor_San_Tekka_brought_before_Kylo_Ren.png/revision/latest?cb=20190604061240) 

Ren hunted Skywalker across the galaxy, searching for clues to the whereabouts of his old master.

 

While Skywalker's location was unknown to the galaxy at large, his old ally, Lor San Tekka, came into possession of a piece of a [star map](/wiki/Star_map "Star map") to the first Jedi Temple some thirty years after the Battle of Endor. When the [Resistance](/wiki/Resistance "Resistance"), a splinter cell of the [New Republic Defense Force](/wiki/New_Republic_Defense_Force "New Republic Defense Force") led by General Leia Organa that [opposed](/wiki/Cold_War "Cold War") the First Order, learned of this, General Organa dispatched [Poe Dameron](/wiki/Poe_Dameron "Poe Dameron") to attempt to retrieve the map from San Tekka's [residence](/wiki/Tuanul "Tuanul") on Jakku. The First Order, however, also seeking Skywalker in an effort to destroy the last of the Jedi, likewise learned of San Tekka's findings and [attacked](/wiki/Attack_on_Tuanul "Attack on Tuanul") Jakku in an effort to retrieve it. An astromech [droid](/wiki/Droid "Droid") named [BB-8](/wiki/BB-8 "BB-8"), with the map in tow, successfully [escaped](/wiki/Escape_from_Jakku "Escape from Jakku") from Jakku with the aid of a Force-sensitive [scavenger](/wiki/Scavenger "Scavenger") named [Rey](/wiki/Rey_Skywalker "Rey Skywalker") and a [First Order stormtrooper](/wiki/First_Order_stormtrooper "First Order stormtrooper") deserter named [Finn](/wiki/Finn "Finn"), who previously helped Dameron escape the First Order's custody. They met and traveled alongside Han Solo and his [Wookiee](/wiki/Wookiee "Wookiee") partner, [Chewbacca](/wiki/Chewbacca "Chewbacca"), in a journey to return BB-8 to the Resistance.[[38]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-38)

 [![During the search for Skywalker, Ren discovered Rey, a Force-sensitive scavenger with a mysterious past.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c3/Rey_vs_Kylo_Ren.png/revision/latest?cb=20160303172711) [![During the search for Skywalker, Ren discovered Rey, a Force-sensitive scavenger with a mysterious past.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c3/Rey_vs_Kylo_Ren.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160303172711)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c3/Rey_vs_Kylo_Ren.png/revision/latest?cb=20160303172711) 

During the search for Skywalker, Ren discovered Rey, a Force-sensitive scavenger with a mysterious past.

 

After a [devastating attack](/wiki/Hosnian_Cataclysm "Hosnian Cataclysm") against the New Republic's capital by the First Order's [Starkiller Base](/wiki/Starkiller_Base "Starkiller Base"), the Resistance sought to [destroy](/wiki/Battle_of_Starkiller_Base "Battle of Starkiller Base") the First Order superweapon. Once there, Han Solo attempted to turn his son back to the light, but he was killed by Ren instead, who was attempting to fully commit to Snoke and the dark side. Rey subsequently defeated Ren in a [lightsaber duel](/wiki/Lightsaber_duel "Lightsaber duel") and Starkiller Base was destroyed, after which the Resistance finally pieced together the map to Skywalker with help from R2-D2. Organa, relieved to finally find her brother, sought to bring him home. She sent Rey, along with Chewbacca and R2-D2, to Ahch-To, where the young girl found Skywalker among the refuge of the first Jedi temple.[[38]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-38)

There, Rey presented the Jedi Master with his [father's lightsaber](/wiki/Skywalker_lightsaber "Skywalker lightsaber")—which [he had lost](/wiki/Duel_on_Cloud_City "Duel on Cloud City") on [Cloud City](/wiki/Cloud_City "Cloud City") decades prior—[[94]](#cite_note-Episode_V-94) as a symbol of the only hope the galaxy had left in defeating Kylo Ren, Snoke, the First Order and Knights of Ren by bringing about the return of the Jedi Order.[[38]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-38)

### Last of the Jedi[]

:   "*The rebellion is reborn today, the war is just beginning, and I will not be the last Jedi.*"
:   ―Luke Skywalker[[18]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-18)

 [![Rey sought out Skywalker, but the Jedi Master was unwilling to train her or help the Resistance.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8b/Rey_returns_lightsaber_TLJ.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180108120250) [![Rey sought out Skywalker, but the Jedi Master was unwilling to train her or help the Resistance.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8b/Rey_returns_lightsaber_TLJ.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180108120250)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8b/Rey_returns_lightsaber_TLJ.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180108120250) 

Rey sought out Skywalker, but the Jedi Master was unwilling to train her or help the Resistance.

 

Rey was surprised to find that Luke Skywalker, the last Jedi, instead rejected her plea for help, tossing his father's lightsaber over his shoulder and confining himself within his hut near the first Jedi Temple. Undeterred, in part thanks to her past as a Jakku scavenger,[[246]](#cite_note-TLJ_Novelization-246) Rey followed Skywalker as he carried on his daily routine despite Skywalker telling her and Chewbacca that he would not face down the First Order. Skywalker was intrigued by Rey, however, when she felt voices calling her through the Force to an [uneti tree](/wiki/Uneti_tree "Uneti tree") containing the sacred Jedi texts. After sneaking aboard the *[Millennium Falcon](/wiki/Millennium_Falcon "Millennium Falcon")* and being shown a [hologram](/wiki/Hologram "Hologram") of his sister's call for help to Jedi General Obi-Wan Kenobi decades earlier by R2-D2, however, Skywalker changed his mind and agreed to teach Rey the ways of the Jedi—and why, in his mind, it was time for the Jedi to end.[[18]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-18)

 [![The bond between Kylo Ren and Rey allowed them to communicate with each other through the Force.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/44/Luke_interrupting_Rey_and_Kylo_Ren.png/revision/latest?cb=20180731154143) [![The bond between Kylo Ren and Rey allowed them to communicate with each other through the Force.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/44/Luke_interrupting_Rey_and_Kylo_Ren.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180731154143)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/44/Luke_interrupting_Rey_and_Kylo_Ren.png/revision/latest?cb=20180731154143) 

The bond between Kylo Ren and Rey allowed them to communicate with each other through the Force.

 

Meanwhile, however, a [Force-bond](/wiki/Force-bond "Force-bond") had opened up between Rey and Kylo Ren, something that Rey decided not to tell her new master. When Skywalker discovered this, he abruptly ended his training of Rey, telling her to leave. After a brief duel, Skywalker finally confessed to Rey the truth of the night his nephew destroyed his fledgling New Jedi Order. Rey, who had grown sympathetic to Ren's conflict over their shared feelings of abandonment, decided to leave Skywalker in an attempt to redeem Ren in the light side, as Skywalker had done to his father decades earlier.[[18]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-18)

Rey traveled to the *[Supremacy](/wiki/Supremacy "Supremacy")*, where Ren took her before his dark side master, Supreme Leader Snoke. Snoke proceeded to use the Force to tortuously probe Rey's mind, finding Skywalker's location. Snoke vowed to obliterate the last Jedi after dealing with the Resistance. Rey defied Snoke, trying to lash out at him; deeming her to have "the spirit of a true Jedi," he commanded Ren to execute Rey. Instead, however, Ren used his grandfather's lightsaber to bisect the Supreme Leader. Ren and Rey then fought Snoke's [Elite Praetorian Guard](/wiki/Praetorian_Guard "Praetorian Guard"), defeating them. However, Ren did not turn back to the light side as Rey believed, rather he usurped his master, fully engrossed in the dark side. Ren offered Rey the chance to rule the galaxy by his side, but instead, the two fought over Skywalker's lightsaber, eventually breaking it in half using the Force, knocking both unconscious.[[18]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-18)

 [![Although Skywalker sacrificed himself for the Resistance, his death did not mark the end of the Jedi.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2e/LukesFinalMoments-TLJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20180421231408) [![Although Skywalker sacrificed himself for the Resistance, his death did not mark the end of the Jedi.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2e/LukesFinalMoments-TLJ.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180421231408)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2e/LukesFinalMoments-TLJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20180421231408) 

Although Skywalker sacrificed himself for the Resistance, his death did not mark the end of the Jedi.

 

After regaining consciousness, Rey escaped the *Supremacy*, regrouping with Chewbacca and R2-D2 above the *Millennium Falcon*. They came to the aid of the Resistance during Ren's [siege of Crait](/wiki/Battle_of_Crait "Battle of Crait")—as did Luke Skywalker. After reuniting with his sister Organa, Skywalker faced his nephew before the [First Order Army](/wiki/First_Order_Army "First Order Army"). However, Skywalker was in fact [projecting](/wiki/Force_projection "Force projection") himself across the galaxy from Ahch-To, buying time for the Resistance's survivors to escape. By the time Ren realized this, it was too late; the remaining survivors of the Resistance, including Poe Dameron, Finn, and Leia Organa, had escaped aboard the *Millennium Falcon* with Chewbacca and Rey, who Skywalker acknowledged as a Jedi. Skywalker's projection disappeared and back at the first Jedi Temple, Skywalker, having exerted a great amount of energy, passed away, becoming one with the Force before the twin suns of Ahch-To. Rey, meanwhile, had recovered Skywalker's lightsaber and began working with the Resistance on the process of building a rebellion against the First Order, while Skywalker's heroic tale spread across the galaxy, inspiring others as the First Order rose to power.[[18]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-18)

### Return and Demise of the Sith Order[]

:   "*I am* all *the Sith!*""*And I… I'm all the Jedi.*"
:   ―Darth Sidious and Rey[[235]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-235)

 [![Darth Sidious returned after his first death to herald the rebirth of the Sith and the ultimate destruction of the Jedi Order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a0/DarthSidiousExegol-TROS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200116140343) [![Darth Sidious returned after his first death to herald the rebirth of the Sith and the ultimate destruction of the Jedi Order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a0/DarthSidiousExegol-TROS.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200116140343)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a0/DarthSidiousExegol-TROS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200116140343) 

Darth Sidious returned after his first death to herald the rebirth of the Sith and the ultimate destruction of the Jedi Order.

 

In the [year](/wiki/35_ABY "35 ABY") following the Battle of [Crait](/wiki/Crait "Crait"), Rey repaired the Skywalker lightsaber continued her Jedi training under Luke Skywalker's twin sister, Leia Organa, who had once briefly trained under her brother as a Jedi herself. Meanwhile, Kylo Ren and the First Order cracked down on any worlds that spread the tale of his defeat at the hands of Luke Skywalker. During that time, a [cult of loyalists](/wiki/Sith_cultist "Sith cultist") to the extinct Sith, the [Sith Eternal](/wiki/Sith_Eternal "Sith Eternal"), revealed themselves to the galaxy from the Unknown Regions by broadcasting the voice of the late Emperor Palpatine, the public identity of Darth Sidious, who was thought to be dead since the Battle of [Endor](/wiki/Endor "Endor"). After [obtaining](/wiki/Mission_to_Mustafar_(First_Order) "Mission to Mustafar (First Order)") a [Sith wayfinder](/wiki/Sith_wayfinder "Sith wayfinder") from [Mustafar](/wiki/Mustafar "Mustafar"), Ren traveled to Exegol and found that Sidious still lived. The Emperor promised Ren the Sith Eternal's fleet of [*Xyston*-class Star Destroyers](/wiki/Xyston-class_Star_Destroyer "Xyston-class Star Destroyer"), the [Final Order](/wiki/Final_Order "Final Order"), if he killed Rey, the last Jedi and the granddaughter of Sidious.[[235]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-235)

After traveling to [Pasaana](/wiki/Mission_to_Pasaana_(Resistance) "Mission to Pasaana (Resistance)") and [Kijimi](/wiki/Mission_to_Kijimi "Mission to Kijimi"), Rey was [confronted](/wiki/Mission_to_Kef_Bir "Mission to Kef Bir") by Ren in the [Death Star ruins](/wiki/Death_Star_ruins "Death Star ruins") on [Kef Bir](/wiki/Kef_Bir "Kef Bir"). Ren, having revealed to Rey her true [lineage](/wiki/Palpatine_family "Palpatine family"), attempted to turn her to the dark side. Their duel was interrupted when Ren sensed his mother's death across the galaxy, allowing Rey to wound the Supreme Leader while he was distracted. After healing Ren, Rey stole his [TIE Whisperer](/wiki/TIE/wi_modified_interceptor "TIE/wi modified interceptor") and returned to the first Jedi Temple on Ahch-To to exile herself as her master had, afraid of her [powers](/wiki/Force_power "Force power") and her potential for the dark side as a descendant of Darth Sidious. The spirit of Luke Skywalker appeared before Rey to motivate and encourage her, teaching his student one last lesson: that confronting fear was the destiny of all Jedi. Skywalker gave Rey his sister's lightsaber and lifted [his](/wiki/Red_Five_(T-65B_X-wing_starfighter) "Red Five (T-65B X-wing starfighter)") [old](/wiki/T-65B_X-wing_starfighter "T-65B X-wing starfighter") [starfighter](/wiki/X-wing_starfighter "X-wing starfighter") out of the Ahch-To seas with the Force, allowing her to use Ren's [wayfinder](/wiki/Wayfinder "Wayfinder") to travel to Exegol. Rey charted her path through hyperspace and transmitted the coordinates to the Resistance, allowing them to travel to Exegol as well.[[235]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-235)

 [![During the Battle of Exegol, Ben Solo and Rey stood together as Jedi against the Sith Emperor.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/71/TheDyadVsTheEmperor-TROS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20250415052905) [![During the Battle of Exegol, Ben Solo and Rey stood together as Jedi against the Sith Emperor.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/71/TheDyadVsTheEmperor-TROS.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250415052905)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/71/TheDyadVsTheEmperor-TROS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20250415052905) 

During the Battle of Exegol, Ben Solo and Rey stood together as Jedi against the Sith Emperor.

 

The [Battle of Exegol](/wiki/Battle_of_Exegol "Battle of Exegol") was fought between the Resistance and the Sith Eternal. It was during the battle that Rey confronted her grandfather Sidious, who offered her the [Throne of the Sith](/wiki/Throne_of_the_Sith "Throne of the Sith") and asked her to take her revenge for having her [father](/wiki/Dathan "Dathan") and [mother](/wiki/Miramir "Miramir") killed by sacrificing him as part of a [ritual](/wiki/Transference "Transference"), allowing the Sith to reborn and ending the Jedi. However, a redeemed Ben Solo, who had renounced the dark side and shed his identity as Kylo Ren, arrived to help Rey. Solo defeated the Knights of Ren, but he and Rey were caught by the Dark Lord of the Sith, who learned that the two were a[[235]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-235) prophesied[[65]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-65) [Force dyad](/wiki/Force_dyad "Force dyad"). Sidious used their bond to heal himself, drawing on their combined life force to restore his body before tossing Solo into a nearby abyss to take his revenge on the [Skywalker family](/wiki/Skywalker_family "Skywalker family") for killing him years earlier at the Battle of Endor. The Sith Lord then unleashed his Force lightning on the Resistance and their [Citizens' Fleet](/wiki/Citizens%27_Fleet "Citizens' Fleet") above. However, Rey was able to reach out to the past Jedi.[[235]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-235) The Jedi Order was gone, but their strength remained.[[4]](#cite_note-DB:Order-4)

 [![The Emperor was destroyed by his granddaughter Rey, who was strengthened by the spirits of the Jedi.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/75/ReyEndsSidious-TROS.png/revision/latest?cb=20250213050821) [![The Emperor was destroyed by his granddaughter Rey, who was strengthened by the spirits of the Jedi.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/75/ReyEndsSidious-TROS.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250213050821)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/75/ReyEndsSidious-TROS.png/revision/latest?cb=20250213050821) 

The Emperor was destroyed by his granddaughter Rey, who was strengthened by the spirits of the Jedi.

 

Upon hearing their voices call to her, Rey was strengthened and rose to face her grandfather. Sidious redirected his Force lightning towards Rey, who defended herself with the lightsabers of her masters. As Sidious boasted that he was all the Sith, Rey responded that she was all the Jedi, and she deflected Sidious's lightning back towards him, causing the Sith Lord to disintegrate and be destroyed at last, preventing the rebirth of the Sith. A massive explosion burst out and erupted, causing the [Sith Citadel](/wiki/Sith_Citadel "Sith Citadel") beneath Exegol to collapse and crumble on the Sith Eternal cultists. Rey sacrificed herself to stop the Emperor, and Solo sacrificed his life in turn to resurrect Rey. With his death, the Skywalker bloodline became extinct.[[235]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-235)

 [![The destruction of the Sith marked a new era in galactic history, to be shaped by the Force in ways as yet unknown.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1c/ReySkywalker.png/revision/latest?cb=20200317091010) [![The destruction of the Sith marked a new era in galactic history, to be shaped by the Force in ways as yet unknown.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1c/ReySkywalker.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/260?cb=20200317091010)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1c/ReySkywalker.png/revision/latest?cb=20200317091010) 

The destruction of the Sith marked a new era in galactic history, to be shaped by the Force in ways as yet unknown.

 

Some time later, Rey buried her mentor's lightsabers at the [Lars moisture farm](/wiki/Lars_homestead "Lars homestead") on Tatooine, the homeworld of the Skywalkers, and unsheathed her own [lightsaber](/wiki/Rey%27s_lightsaber "Rey's lightsaber"). When a [local elderly woman](/wiki/Unidentified_Tatooine_elder "Unidentified Tatooine elder") stumbled upon Rey using her lightsaber, she asked the scavenger her name. Seeing the spirits of Luke and Leia in the distance, Rey responded that she was "Rey Skywalker."[[235]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-235)
In the aftermath of the First Order/Resistance War, Rey eventually gained the status of Jedi Master while fighting to restore galactic peace. As Master, Rey started to work on rebuilding the Jedi Order.[[20]](#cite_note-TSWB-20)

### Legacy[]

:   "*Now that they're extinct, the Jedi are romanticized, deified. But if you strip away the myth and look at their deeds, the legacy of the Jedi is failure. Hypocrisy, hubris…*"  
    "*That's not true.*"  
    "*At the height of their powers, they allowed Darth Sidious to rise, create the Empire, and wipe them out. It was a Jedi Master who was responsible for the training and creation of Darth Vader.*"  
    "*And a Jedi who saved him.*"
:   ―Luke Skywalker and Rey[[18]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-18)

 [![The Jedi Order was mythologized after its extinction, surviving in memory as a symbol of hope in the galaxy.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/80/JediOrder-SOTJ.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210702151017) [![The Jedi Order was mythologized after its extinction, surviving in memory as a symbol of hope in the galaxy.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/80/JediOrder-SOTJ.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20210702151017)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/80/JediOrder-SOTJ.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210702151017) 

The Jedi Order was mythologized after its extinction, surviving in memory as a symbol of hope in the galaxy.

 

After the fall of the Empire, the Jedi Order's memory was rehabilitated and mythologized. The Jedi were romanticized during the New Republic Era, becoming deified symbols of a bygone era. Despite the Order's extinction, Supreme Leader Snoke endeavored to eradicate all traces of its past, believing that the Jedi inspired hope in the enemies of the First Order.[[18]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-18)

Luke Skywalker, a legendary Jedi Master, devoted years to rediscovering the Order’s history which he chronicled in the book ‘’[The Secrets of the Jedi](/wiki/The_Secrets_of_the_Jedi "The Secrets of the Jedi")‘’. Although Skywalker held individual Jedi, such as Mace Windu, Yoda, or Qui-Gon Jinn, in high esteem,[[62]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Jedi-62) he became disillusioned by the Order’s failure toward the end of its history prior to the rise of the Empire. He faulted the Order for not thwarting the machinations of Darth Sidious, causing the extinction of the Jedi. Skywalker also believed that his old mentor, Obi-Wan Kenobi, was responsible for his father’s transformation into Darth Vader. Later, to Rey, Skywalker admitted that he was wrong and encouraged her to keep the Jedi way and fight Sidious.[[155]](#cite_note-TROS_JN-155) After his faith in the Jedi was restored by Rey and Yoda, Skywalker’s final stand allowed the legend of the Jedi to spread once more, bringing hope to the galaxy.[[18]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-18)

## Behind the scenes[]

### Development and portrayal[]

The Jedi Order (as formal organization, not just scattered survivors) first appeared in the current [canon](/wiki/Canon "Canon") in [*Star Wars*: Episode I *The Phantom Menace*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_I_The_Phantom_Menace "Star Wars: Episode I The Phantom Menace"), though it previously appeared in various [*Star Wars* Legends](/wiki/Star_Wars_Legends "Star Wars Legends") sources beforehand. The lore of the Jedi Order and of the Force was greatly expanded upon during the *[Star Wars: The Clone Wars](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Clone_Wars "Star Wars: The Clone Wars")* television series and other media. The role of the Jedi Order in preserving the peace of the Republic, the controversy of them stepping into the role of military leaders, and their rules against attachment in order to keep to the light are pivotal plot points that Darth Sidious all exploits, which eventually leads to the Order's downfall in [*Star Wars*: Episode III *Revenge of the Sith*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_III_Revenge_of_the_Sith "Star Wars: Episode III Revenge of the Sith"). Prior to that, they had been mentioned indirectly as the Jedi in the original trilogy as Luke Skywalker encounters Jedi Master Obi-Wan Kenobi and later Master Yoda. In [*Star Wars*: Episode VI *Return of the Jedi*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_VI_Return_of_the_Jedi "Star Wars: Episode VI Return of the Jedi"), Yoda charges Luke with carrying on the lessons and legacy of the Jedi Order.

For the word "Jedi," Lucas took inspiration from the [Japanese](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Japanese_language "wikipedia:Japanese language") term "[Jidaigeki](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jidaigeki "wikipedia:Jidaigeki")," which refers to a drama set during the [Edo period](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edo_period "wikipedia:Edo period") of Japanese history, when [samurai](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Samurai "wikipedia:Samurai") were still in activity.[[247]](#cite_note-Scrap-247) The word "Jedi" is a singular plural.[[248]](#cite_note-Plural-248) The Jedi Order originated in the rough draft of *Star Wars* as the Galactic Emperor's [bodyguard](/wiki/Bodyguard "Bodyguard"). They became affiliated with the *[Republica Galactica](/wiki/Republica_Galactica "Republica Galactica")* in the second draft.[[249]](#cite_note-Empire_DB-249) Later, when composing background information for licensees in [1977](/wiki/1977 "1977"), [George Lucas](/wiki/George_Lucas "George Lucas") described the Jedi Order as being "several hundred thousand" strong before the Purge.[[250]](#cite_note-The_Making_of_Star_Wars:_The_Definitive_Story_Behind_the_Original_Film-250)

### Prequel trilogy and *The Clone Wars*[]
